<div class="toast" id="toast"></div>

<script>
const STORE='tendedV4', SALT_KEY='tendedSalt', ENC_KEY='tendedEncKey';
let D={meds:[],appts:[],health:[],symptoms:[],claims:[],docs:[],family:[],contacts:[],settings:{},medChecks:{},notifications:[],prepChecks:{},checkins:[]};
let _cryptoKey=null, _encReady=false;

// ── AES-256-GCM Encryption ────────────────────────────────────────
async function deriveKey(pin, salt){
  const enc=new TextEncoder();
  const base=await crypto.subtle.importKey('raw',enc.encode(pin),'PBKDF2',false,['deriveKey']);
  return crypto.subtle.deriveKey({name:'PBKDF2',salt,iterations:200000,hash:'SHA-256'},base,{name:'AES-GCM',length:256},false,['encrypt','decrypt']);
}
async function encryptData(plain,key){
  const iv=crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(12));
  const ct=await crypto.subtle.encrypt({name:'AES-GCM',iv},key,new TextEncoder().encode(plain));
  const buf=new Uint8Array(12+ct.byteLength);buf.set(iv);buf.set(new Uint8Array(ct),12);
  return btoa(String.fromCharCode(...buf));
}
async function decryptData(b64,key){
  const buf=Uint8Array.from(atob(b64),c=>c.charCodeAt(0));
  const pt=await crypto.subtle.decrypt({name:'AES-GCM',iv:buf.slice(0,12)},key,buf.slice(12));
  return new TextDecoder().decode(pt);
}
async function hashPin(pin){
  const enc=new TextEncoder();
  const h=await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256',enc.encode('tended_salt_'+pin));
  return btoa(String.fromCharCode(...new Uint8Array(h)));
}
async function verifyPin(pin){
  const stored=localStorage.getItem('tendedPinHash');
  if(!stored)return false;
  const h=await hashPin(pin);
  return h===stored;
}
async function initEncryption(pin){
  let saltB64=localStorage.getItem(SALT_KEY);
  let salt;
  if(!saltB64){salt=crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(32));localStorage.setItem(SALT_KEY,btoa(String.fromCharCode(...salt)));}
  else salt=Uint8Array.from(atob(saltB64),c=>c.charCodeAt(0));
  _cryptoKey=await deriveKey(pin,salt);
  _encReady=true;
}
async function saveEncrypted(){
  // Always save plaintext first — this is the reliable source on reload
  try{ localStorage.setItem(STORE, JSON.stringify(D)); } catch(e){}
  // Also save encrypted copy if PIN is active (bonus security layer)
  if(_encReady && _cryptoKey){
    try{
      const enc = await encryptData(JSON.stringify(D), _cryptoKey);
      localStorage.setItem(STORE+'_enc', enc);
    }catch(e){}
  }
}
async function loadEncrypted(pin){
  // Primary: always load from plaintext store (always current, always available)
  try{
    const s=localStorage.getItem(STORE);
    if(s) D=Object.assign(D, JSON.parse(s));
  }catch(e){}
  // Secondary: init encryption key so future saves are also encrypted
  if(pin){
    try{ await initEncryption(pin); }catch(e){}
  }
  return true;
}

// save() calls async saveEncrypted — always writes to localStorage
function save(){ saveEncrypted(); }
// Initial load on startup — read from localStorage immediately
try{
  const _s = localStorage.getItem(STORE);
  if(_s) D = Object.assign(D, JSON.parse(_s));
}catch(e){}

function fmtDate(d){try{return new Date(d+'T00:00:00').toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'});}catch{return d;}}
function fmtTime(t){try{return new Date('1970-01-01T'+t).toLocaleTimeString('en-US',{hour:'numeric',minute:'2-digit'});}catch{return t;}}
function parseTime(s){const m=s.match(/(\d+):(\d+)\s*(AM|PM)/i);if(!m)return s.toLowerCase().includes('bed')?82800000:0;let h=parseInt(m[1]),mn=parseInt(m[2]);if(m[3].toUpperCase()==='PM'&&h!==12)h+=12;if(m[3].toUpperCase()==='AM'&&h===12)h=0;return h*3600000+mn*60000;}
function clearInputs(ids){ids.forEach(id=>{const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.value=''});}
function toast(msg,color='var(--slate)'){const t=document.getElementById('toast');t.textContent=msg;t.style.background=color;t.classList.add('show');setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove('show'),2800);}
function openModal(id){document.getElementById(id).classList.add('open');}
function closeModal(id, force=false){
  const overlay = document.getElementById(id);
  if(!force && overlay){
    const modal = overlay.querySelector('.modal');
    if(modal && modal.classList.contains('dirty')){
      if(!confirm('Discard unsaved changes?')) return;
    }
    if(modal) modal.classList.remove('dirty');
  }
  if(overlay) overlay.classList.remove('open');
}
function markModalDirty(id){
  const m = document.getElementById(id)?.querySelector('.modal');
  if(m) m.classList.add('dirty');
}
document.querySelectorAll('.overlay').forEach(o=>o.addEventListener('click',function(e){if(e.target===this)this.classList.remove('open');}));

// Display Mode
function applyDisplayMode(){
  const dark=document.getElementById('toggle-dark')?.checked;
  const large=document.getElementById('toggle-large')?.checked;
  const contrast=document.getElementById('toggle-contrast')?.checked;
  document.body.classList.toggle('dark-mode',!!dark);
  document.body.classList.toggle('large-text',!!large);
  document.body.classList.toggle('high-contrast',!!contrast);
  D.settings.displayDark=dark;D.settings.displayLarge=large;D.settings.displayContrast=contrast;save();
}
function loadDisplayMode(){
  const s=D.settings;
  ['toggle-dark','toggle-large','toggle-contrast'].forEach((id,i)=>{const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.checked=!![s.displayDark,s.displayLarge,s.displayContrast][i];});
  document.body.classList.toggle('dark-mode',!!s.displayDark);
  document.body.classList.toggle('large-text',!!s.displayLarge);
  document.body.classList.toggle('high-contrast',!!s.displayContrast);
  syncDarkBtn();
}

// PIN
const PIN_KEY='tendedPin',PIN_SET='tendedPinSet',CG_PIN_KEY='tendedCgPin';
let pinBuffer='',pinMode='enter',pinFirst='',caregiverMode=false;
function initPin(){
  const set  = localStorage.getItem(PIN_SET);
  const hash = localStorage.getItem('tendedPinHash');

  // No PIN ever configured OR explicitly disabled → go straight in
  if(!set || set === 'disabled'){
    unlockApp(null);
    return;
  }

  // PIN flagged as set but no hash stored = stale/corrupt state
  // (happens when testing or migrating from an old version)
  // Treat as no PIN and go straight in — user can set a new one in Settings
  if(set === '1' && !hash){
    localStorage.setItem(PIN_SET, 'disabled');
    unlockApp(null);
    return;
  }

  // PIN is set and hash exists — show the lock screen
  document.getElementById('pin-screen').style.display = 'flex';
  document.getElementById('pin-title').textContent    = 'Tended';
  document.getElementById('pin-subtitle').textContent = 'Enter your PIN to continue';
  document.getElementById('pin-forgot').style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('pin-skip-btn').style.display = 'none';
  pinMode = 'enter';

  // Offer biometric if enrolled
  if(localStorage.getItem('tendedBioOn')){
    const b = document.getElementById('pin-bio-btn');
    if(b){ b.style.display = 'block'; }
    setTimeout(async()=>{ await bioUnlock(); }, 400);
  }
}
function skipPin(){
  localStorage.setItem(PIN_SET,'disabled');
  unlockApp(null);
}
function pinPress(d){if(pinBuffer.length>=4)return;pinBuffer+=d;updateDots();document.getElementById('pin-error').textContent='';if(pinBuffer.length===4)setTimeout(pinSubmit,120);}
function pinClear(){pinBuffer=pinBuffer.slice(0,-1);updateDots();}
function pinAction(){if(pinBuffer.length===4)pinSubmit();}
function updateDots(){for(let i=0;i<4;i++)document.getElementById('dot-'+i).classList.toggle('filled',i<pinBuffer.length);}
function pinSubmit(){
  if(pinMode==='setup'){pinFirst=pinBuffer;pinBuffer='';updateDots();pinMode='confirm';document.getElementById('pin-subtitle').textContent='Confirm your PIN';
    document.getElementById('pin-skip-btn').style.display='none';return;}
  if(pinMode==='confirm'){
    if(pinBuffer===pinFirst){const pinVal=pinBuffer;hashPin(pinVal).then(h=>{localStorage.setItem(PIN_KEY,h);localStorage.setItem('tendedPinHash',h);localStorage.setItem(PIN_SET,'1');unlockApp(pinVal);toast('✅ PIN created!','var(--sage)');});}
    else{pinError("PINs don't match — try again");pinMode='setup';pinFirst='';document.getElementById('pin-subtitle').textContent='Create a PIN — or skip to enter without one';
      document.getElementById('pin-skip-btn').style.display='block';}
    return;
  }
  // Verify PIN using SHA-256 hash (matches how it was stored)
  const _pv = pinBuffer;
  verifyPin(_pv).then(ok => {
    if(ok) unlockApp(_pv);
    else {
      // Legacy fallback: some older installs used plain btoa storage
      const legacy = localStorage.getItem(PIN_KEY);
      if(legacy && _pv === atob(legacy)) unlockApp(_pv);
      else pinError('Incorrect PIN — try again');
    }
  });
}
function pinError(msg){pinBuffer='';updateDots();document.getElementById('pin-error').textContent=msg;document.querySelectorAll('.pin-dot').forEach(d=>{d.classList.add('shake');setTimeout(()=>d.classList.remove('shake'),400);});}
function unlockApp(pin){
  document.getElementById('pin-screen').style.display='none';
  if(localStorage.getItem(PIN_SET)==='1'){
    resetLockTimer();
    document.addEventListener('click',resetLockTimer);
    document.addEventListener('keydown',resetLockTimer);
    if(pin) initEncryption(pin).then(()=>{
      const plain=localStorage.getItem(STORE);
      if(plain&&!localStorage.getItem(STORE+'_enc')) saveEncrypted();
    });
    // Show lock button when PIN is active
    const lb = document.getElementById('lock-now-btn');
    if(lb) lb.style.display = 'flex';
  }
  // Show onboarding for genuine new users (no data, never onboarded)
  const isNew = !localStorage.getItem(OB_DONE_KEY) && !D.meds.length && !D.appts.length && !D.health.length;
  if(isNew){ setTimeout(obShow, 350); }
  else { showCheckinIfNeeded(); }
}

function lockNow(){
  // Clear inactivity timer
  clearTimeout(lockTimer);
  // Reset PIN screen to enter mode
  pinBuffer = ''; pinMode = 'enter'; updateDots();
  document.getElementById('pin-subtitle').textContent = 'Enter your PIN to continue';
  document.getElementById('pin-error').textContent = '';
  document.getElementById('pin-forgot').style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('pin-skip-btn').style.display = 'none';
  // Show biometric button if enrolled
  const bioBtn = document.getElementById('pin-bio-btn');
  if(bioBtn) bioBtn.style.display = localStorage.getItem('tendedBioOn') ? 'block' : 'none';
  // Lock
  document.getElementById('pin-screen').style.display = 'flex';
}
const LOCK_TIMEOUT_KEY = 'tendedLockTimeout';
function getLockTimeoutMs(){
  const mins = parseInt(localStorage.getItem(LOCK_TIMEOUT_KEY)||'10');
  return mins === 0 ? 0 : mins * 60 * 1000;
}
function saveLockTimeout(val){
  localStorage.setItem(LOCK_TIMEOUT_KEY, val);
  clearTimeout(lockTimer);
  if(parseInt(val) > 0) resetLockTimer();
}
function loadLockTimeout(){
  const val = localStorage.getItem(LOCK_TIMEOUT_KEY)||'10';
  const sel = document.getElementById('lock-timeout-sel');
  if(sel) sel.value = val;
}
let lockTimer;
function resetLockTimer(){
  clearTimeout(lockTimer);
  const ms = getLockTimeoutMs();
  if(ms === 0) return; // "Never" selected
  lockTimer=setTimeout(()=>{
    if(localStorage.getItem(PIN_SET)!=='1') return;
    pinBuffer='';pinMode='enter';updateDots();
    document.getElementById('pin-subtitle').textContent='Enter your PIN to continue';
    document.getElementById('pin-error').textContent='';
    document.getElementById('pin-skip-btn').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('pin-forgot').style.display='block';
    document.getElementById('pin-screen').style.display='flex';
  }, ms);
}
function pinForgot(){
  if(!confirm('This will delete ALL your health data and remove the PIN. Are you sure?')) return;
  if(!confirm('Last chance — this cannot be undone. Delete everything?')) return;
  // Clear all app keys
  ['tendedV4','tendedV4_enc','tendedSalt','tendedPin','tendedPinSet','tendedPinHash',
   'tendedOnboarded','tendedProfiles','tendedActiveProfile','tendedBioId','tendedBioOn',
   'tendedApiKey','tendedCgPin','lifeAdminV3_cgShare','_authToken','_authRefresh','_authExpiresAt',
   'tendedTourDone','tendedLockTimeout'
  ].forEach(k => localStorage.removeItem(k));
  // Explicitly disable PIN so the next load goes straight to the app
  localStorage.setItem('tendedPinSet','disabled');
  location.reload();
}
function changePinFlow(){
  pinBuffer=''; pinFirst=''; pinMode='setup'; updateDots();
  document.getElementById('pin-title').textContent = 'Change PIN';
  document.getElementById('pin-subtitle').textContent = 'Create a new 4-digit PIN';
  document.getElementById('pin-forgot').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('pin-skip-btn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('pin-error').textContent = '';
  document.getElementById('pin-screen').style.display = 'flex';
}
function disablePin(){
  if(!confirm('Remove PIN lock? The app will open without asking for a PIN.')) return;
  localStorage.setItem(PIN_SET, 'disabled');
  localStorage.removeItem(PIN_KEY);
  localStorage.removeItem('tendedPinHash');
  localStorage.removeItem('tendedBioId');
  localStorage.removeItem('tendedBioOn');
  clearTimeout(lockTimer);
  renderPinStatus();
  toast('PIN removed — app will open directly', 'var(--sage)');
}

// Caregiver
function saveCaregiverPin(){const v=document.getElementById('cg-pin-input').value.trim();if(v.length!==4||isNaN(v)){toast('Please enter exactly 4 digits','var(--amber)');return;}localStorage.setItem(CG_PIN_KEY,btoa(v));toast('✅ Caregiver PIN saved!','var(--sage)');}
function enterCaregiverMode(){
  const input=document.getElementById('cg-pin-input').value.trim();const stored=localStorage.getItem(CG_PIN_KEY);
  if(!stored){toast('Please create a Caregiver PIN first','var(--amber)');return;}
  if(input!==atob(stored)){toast('Incorrect Caregiver PIN','#DC2626');return;}
  caregiverMode=true;document.getElementById('caregiver-banner').classList.add('show');
  document.querySelectorAll('.no-caregiver').forEach(el=>el.style.display='none');
  renderCgPreview();navTo('dashboard');toast('👁 Caregiver view active','#7C3AED');
}
function exitCaregiverMode(){caregiverMode=false;document.getElementById('caregiver-banner').classList.remove('show');document.querySelectorAll('.no-caregiver').forEach(el=>el.style.display='');}
function renderCgPreview(){
  const el=document.getElementById('cg-preview');if(!el)return;
  const today=new Date().toDateString();const done=D.meds.filter(m=>D.medChecks[m.id+'_'+today]).length;
  const upcoming=D.appts.filter(a=>new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00')>=new Date()).slice(0,2);const lv=D.health[0];
  el.innerHTML=`<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px;margin-bottom:14px">
    <div style="background:var(--teal-pale);border:1.5px solid var(--teal-mid);border-radius:10px;padding:14px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:1.6rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--teal)">${done}/${D.meds.length}</div><div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--teal)">Meds taken today</div></div>
    <div style="background:var(--indigo-pale);border:1.5px solid #C7D2FE;border-radius:10px;padding:14px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:1.6rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--indigo)">${upcoming.length}</div><div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--indigo)">Upcoming appts</div></div>
  </div>${lv?`<div style="background:var(--cream);border:1.5px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;padding:12px;font-size:.85rem"><strong>Latest vitals</strong> (${fmtDate(lv.date)})<div style="margin-top:6px;display:flex;gap:12px;flex-wrap:wrap">${lv.bp?`<span>🩺 ${lv.bp}</span>`:''}${lv.hr?`<span>💓 ${lv.hr} bpm</span>`:''}${lv.wt?`<span>⚖️ ${lv.wt} lbs</span>`:''}</div></div>`:''}
  ${upcoming.length?`<div style="margin-top:12px">${upcoming.map(a=>`<div style="font-size:.85rem;margin-top:6px;padding:8px;background:var(--indigo-pale);border-radius:8px">📅 ${fmtDate(a.date)} — ${a.name}</div>`).join('')}</div>`:''}`;
}

// Check-in
let checkinFeel=0;
function showCheckinIfNeeded(){const today=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];if(!D.checkins)D.checkins=[];if(!D.checkins.find(c=>c.date===today))setTimeout(()=>document.getElementById('checkin-overlay').style.display='flex',800);}
function openCheckin(){document.getElementById('checkin-overlay').style.display='flex';}
function selectCheckinFeel(v,btn){checkinFeel=v;document.querySelectorAll('.feel-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('sel'));btn.classList.add('sel');}
function submitCheckin(){
  if(!checkinFeel){toast('Please select how you feel','var(--amber)');return;}
  const today=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];if(!D.checkins)D.checkins=[];
  D.checkins=D.checkins.filter(c=>c.date!==today);
  D.checkins.unshift({date:today,feel:checkinFeel,notes:document.getElementById('checkin-notes').value,ts:Date.now()});
  if(!D.health.find(h=>h.date===today)){D.health.unshift({id:Date.now(),date:today,bp:'',hr:'',wt:'',bs:'',temp:'',o2:'',feel:String(checkinFeel),notes:document.getElementById('checkin-notes').value});D.health.sort((a,b)=>new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date));}
  save();document.getElementById('checkin-overlay').style.display='none';document.getElementById('checkin-notes').value='';checkinFeel=0;document.querySelectorAll('.feel-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('sel'));
  renderCheckinStrip();renderAll();toast('✅ Check-in saved!','var(--sage)');
}
function skipCheckin(){document.getElementById('checkin-overlay').style.display='none';}
function renderCheckinStrip(){
  const strip=document.getElementById('checkin-strip');const today=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  const ci=D.checkins&&D.checkins.find(c=>c.date===today);
  if(!ci){strip.style.display='none';return;}
  const fe={5:'😄 Great',4:'🙂 Good',3:'😐 Okay',2:'😕 Not great',1:'😞 Rough'};
  strip.style.display='block';
  strip.innerHTML=`<div style="background:var(--teal-pale);border:1.5px solid var(--teal-mid);border-radius:var(--r);padding:14px 20px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:14px"><span style="font-size:1.6rem">${['','😞','😕','😐','🙂','😄'][ci.feel]}</span><div><strong>Today's check-in:</strong> Feeling ${fe[ci.feel]||''}${ci.notes?' — '+ci.notes:''}</div><button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" style="margin-left:auto" onclick="openCheckin()">Update</button></div>`;
}

// API Key
const AK='tendedApiKey';
function getApiKey(){return localStorage.getItem(AK)||'';}
function saveApiKey(k){localStorage.setItem(AK,k.trim());}
function showApiKeyPrompt(){document.getElementById('apikey-overlay').style.display='flex';}
function closeApiKeyPrompt(){document.getElementById('apikey-overlay').style.display='none';}
function submitApiKey(){const v=document.getElementById('apikey-input').value.trim();if(!v.startsWith('sk-ant-')){toast('Key should start with sk-ant-','#B45309');return;}saveApiKey(v);closeApiKeyPrompt();toast('✅ API key saved!','var(--sage)');renderKeyStatus();}
function clearApiKey(){localStorage.removeItem(AK);document.getElementById('apikey-input').value='';}
function renderKeyStatus(){const el=document.getElementById('key-status');if(!el)return;el.innerHTML=getApiKey()?'<span style="color:var(--sage)">✅ API key set — AI features active</span>':'<span style="color:var(--slate-light)">⚪ No API key — AI disabled</span>';}
async function apiFetch(body){
  const key=getApiKey();if(!key){showApiKeyPrompt();throw new Error('NO_KEY');}
  const r=await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json','x-api-key':key,'anthropic-version':'2023-06-01','anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access':'true'},body:JSON.stringify(body)});
  if(r.status===401){showApiKeyPrompt();throw new Error('INVALID_KEY');}
  return r.json();
}

// NOTIFICATIONS & BACKGROUND REMINDERS

// ── In-app notification panel ─────────────────────────────────────
function addNotif(icon, title, body){
  D.notifications.unshift({id:Date.now(),ts:Date.now(),icon,title,body,
    time:new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US',{hour:'numeric',minute:'2-digit'})});
  if(D.notifications.length > 30) D.notifications.pop();
  save(); renderNotifBadge();
}
function renderNotifBadge(){ document.getElementById('notif-dot').style.display = D.notifications.length ? 'block' : 'none'; }
function toggleNotifPanel(){ document.getElementById('notif-panel').classList.toggle('open'); renderNotifList(); }
function renderNotifList(){
  const list = document.getElementById('notif-list');
  if(!D.notifications.length){ list.innerHTML='<div style="padding:16px;color:var(--slate-light);text-align:center">No notifications</div>'; return; }
  list.innerHTML = D.notifications.map(n =>
    `<div class="notif-item"><div style="font-size:1.3rem;flex-shrink:0">${n.icon}</div><div><strong>${n.title}</strong><div>${n.body}</div><div class="notif-time">${n.time}</div></div></div>`
  ).join('');
}
function clearNotifs(){ D.notifications=[]; save(); renderNotifBadge(); renderNotifList(); }
document.addEventListener('click', e => {
  const p = document.getElementById('notif-panel');
  const t = document.getElementById('notif-trigger');
  if(!p.contains(e.target) && !t.contains(e.target)) p.classList.remove('open');
});

// ── Push to service worker schedule ─────────────────────────────────

// ── Request permission + enable reminders ─────────────────────────

// ── Checkup alerts on launch ──────────────────────────────────────
function checkRefillAlerts(){
  D.meds.forEach(m => {
    if(!m.refill) return;
    const days = Math.ceil((new Date(m.refill+'T00:00:00') - new Date()) / 86400000);
    if(days <= 7 && days >= 0){
      const msg = days === 0 ? 'Due today — call the pharmacy!' : `Due in ${days} day${days!==1?'s':''}`;
      addNotif('📦', `Refill needed: ${m.name}`, msg);
    }
  });
}

function checkApptAlerts(){
  const tm = new Date(); tm.setDate(tm.getDate()+1);
  const ts = tm.toISOString().split('T')[0];
  const td = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  D.appts.forEach(a => {
    if(a.date === ts) addNotif('📅','Appointment tomorrow',`${a.name}${a.time?' at '+fmtTime(a.time):''}`);
    if(a.date === td) addNotif('📅','Appointment TODAY',`${a.name}${a.time?' at '+fmtTime(a.time):''}${a.loc?' · '+a.loc:''}`);
  });
}

// Multi-Profile
const PROFILE_STORE='tendedProfiles',ACTIVE_PROFILE='tendedActiveProfile';
let profiles=[],activeProfileId='default',selProfileColor='#0F766E';
function loadProfiles(){
  try{const p=localStorage.getItem(PROFILE_STORE);if(p)profiles=JSON.parse(p);}catch(e){}
  if(!profiles.length){profiles=[{id:'default',name:D.settings.name||'My Profile',rel:'Myself',dob:D.settings.dob||'',color:'#0F766E',created:Date.now()}];saveProfiles();}
  activeProfileId=localStorage.getItem(ACTIVE_PROFILE)||'default';
}
function saveProfiles(){try{localStorage.setItem(PROFILE_STORE,JSON.stringify(profiles));}catch(e){}}
function selectProfileColor(el){selProfileColor=el.dataset.color;document.querySelectorAll('[data-color]').forEach(s=>s.style.borderColor='transparent');el.style.borderColor='white';}
function addProfile(){
  const name=document.getElementById('prof-name').value.trim();if(!name){toast('Please enter a name');return;}
  const id='prof_'+Date.now();
  profiles.push({id,name,rel:document.getElementById('prof-rel').value,dob:document.getElementById('prof-dob').value,color:selProfileColor,created:Date.now()});
  localStorage.setItem('tendedV4_'+id,JSON.stringify({meds:[],appts:[],health:[],symptoms:[],claims:[],docs:[],family:[],contacts:[],settings:{name},medChecks:{},notifications:[],prepChecks:{},checkins:[]}));
  saveProfiles();closeModal('profile-modal');clearInputs(['prof-name','prof-dob']);renderProfiles();toast('✅ Profile created!','var(--sage)');
}
function switchProfile(id){
  localStorage.setItem('tendedV4_'+activeProfileId,JSON.stringify(D));
  activeProfileId=id;localStorage.setItem(ACTIVE_PROFILE,id);
  try{const key=id==='default'?STORE:'tendedV4_'+id;const s=localStorage.getItem(key);if(s)D=Object.assign({meds:[],appts:[],health:[],symptoms:[],claims:[],docs:[],family:[],contacts:[],settings:{},medChecks:{},notifications:[],prepChecks:{},checkins:[]},JSON.parse(s));}catch(e){}
  loadSettings();loadDisplayMode();renderAll();
  const prof=profiles.find(p=>p.id===id);toast(`Switched to ${prof?.name||'profile'}`,'var(--teal)');
  document.getElementById('user-name-chip').textContent=D.settings.name||prof?.name||'Profile';
}
function deleteProfile(id){if(id==='default'){toast('Cannot delete the main profile');return;}if(!confirm('Delete this profile and all its data?'))return;profiles=profiles.filter(p=>p.id!==id);localStorage.removeItem('tendedV4_'+id);saveProfiles();if(activeProfileId===id)switchProfile('default');renderProfiles();toast('Profile deleted');}
function renderProfiles(){
  const grid=document.getElementById('profiles-grid');if(!grid)return;
  grid.innerHTML=profiles.map(p=>{const isActive=p.id===activeProfileId;return`<div class="card" style="border:2px solid ${isActive?p.color:'var(--border)'}"><div style="width:48px;height:48px;border-radius:50%;background:${p.color};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:1.5rem;margin-bottom:12px">👤</div><div style="font-weight:700;font-size:1rem">${p.name}</div><div style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-light);margin-top:3px">${p.rel}${p.dob?' · '+p.dob:''}</div>${isActive?`<div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:700;color:${p.color};margin-top:6px">● Active</div>`:''}<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:14px">${!isActive?`<button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="switchProfile('${p.id}')" style="background:${p.color}">Switch</button>`:'<button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" disabled>Current</button>'}${p.id!=='default'?`<button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="deleteProfile('${p.id}')">✕</button>`:''}</div></div>`;}).join('');
}

// QR Card
function generateQrCard(){
  if(!D.settings.name){toast('Please set your name in Settings first','var(--amber)');return;}
  const meds=D.meds.slice(0,8).map(m=>`${m.name} ${m.dose||''}`).join(', ')||'None';
  // Use flagged contacts first, fall back to first 3 if none flagged
  const qrConts = D.contacts.filter(c=>c.onQR).length ? D.contacts.filter(c=>c.onQR) : D.contacts.slice(0,3);
  const contacts = qrConts.map(c=>`${c.name}: ${c.phone}`).join(' | ')||'None';
  const lv=D.health[0];const vitals=lv?`BP:${lv.bp||'?'} HR:${lv.hr||'?'} Wt:${lv.wt||'?'}lbs`:'Not recorded';
  const allergies = [
    D.settings.drugAllergies  ? 'Drug: '  + D.settings.drugAllergies  : '',
    D.settings.foodAllergies  ? 'Food: '  + D.settings.foodAllergies  : '',
    D.settings.otherAllergies ? 'Other: ' + D.settings.otherAllergies : ''
  ].filter(Boolean).join(' | ') || 'None known';
  const conditions = (typeof D.settings.conditions==='string' ? D.settings.conditions : (D.settings.conditions||[]).join(', ')) || 'None listed';
  const text=[`TENDED EMERGENCY CARD`,`Name: ${D.settings.name}`,`DOB: ${D.settings.dob||'Not set'}`,`Blood Type: ${D.settings.blood||'Unknown'}`,`Doctor: ${D.settings.doc||'Not set'}`,`Phone: ${D.settings.phone||'Not set'}`,`ALLERGIES: ${allergies}`,`CONDITIONS: ${conditions}`,`Medications: ${meds}`,`Vitals: ${vitals}`,`Emergency Contacts: ${contacts}`,`Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}`].join('\n');
  const qrUrl=`https://api.qrserver.com/v1/create-qr-code/?size=220x220&data=${encodeURIComponent(text)}`;
  document.getElementById('qr-container').innerHTML=`<img src="${qrUrl}" style="border-radius:10px;border:3px solid var(--teal)" alt="Emergency QR Code" onerror="this.parentElement.innerHTML='<div style=padding:20px;color:var(--rose)>Requires internet connection.</div>'">`;
  const allergyHtml = [
    D.settings.drugAllergies  ? '<span style="color:var(--rose)">💊 Drug: ' + D.settings.drugAllergies  + '</span>' : '',
    D.settings.foodAllergies  ? '<span style="color:var(--amber)">🍽️ Food: '  + D.settings.foodAllergies  + '</span>' : '',
    D.settings.otherAllergies ? 'Other: ' + D.settings.otherAllergies : ''
  ].filter(Boolean).join('<br>') || 'None known';
  const condHtml = (typeof D.settings.conditions==='string' ? D.settings.conditions : (D.settings.conditions||[]).join(', ')) || 'None listed';
  document.getElementById('qr-preview').innerHTML=`<strong>${D.settings.name}</strong><br>DOB: ${D.settings.dob||'Not set'}&nbsp;&nbsp;Blood Type: ${D.settings.blood||'Unknown'}<br>Doctor: ${D.settings.doc||'Not set'}<br>Phone: ${D.settings.phone||'Not set'}<br><br><strong>⚠️ Allergies:</strong><br>${allergyHtml}<br><br><strong>🏥 Conditions:</strong><br>${condHtml}<br><br><strong>Medications:</strong> ${meds}<br><br><strong>Vitals:</strong> ${vitals}<br><br><strong>Emergency Contacts:</strong><br>${contacts.replace(/\|/g,'<br>')}`;
  toast('✅ QR card generated!','var(--sage)');
}
function printQrCard(){
  const container=document.getElementById('qr-container');
  if(!container.querySelector('img')){generateQrCard();setTimeout(printQrCard,1500);return;}
  const w=window.open('','_blank');w.document.write(`<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><title>Emergency Card</title><style>body{font-family:Georgia,serif;max-width:400px;margin:40px auto;text-align:center;font-size:14px}h2{color:#0F766E}.card{border:3px solid #0F766E;border-radius:12px;padding:20px;margin-top:16px}.info{text-align:left;margin-top:16px;line-height:1.9}
.bn-menu-item{display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:6px;padding:14px 10px;border:1.5px solid var(--border);border-radius:12px;background:var(--cream);cursor:pointer;font-family:'DM Sans',sans-serif;font-size:1.4rem;transition:all .15s}

// Health Summary
function buildSummaryPreview(){
  const el=document.getElementById('summary-preview');if(!el)return;
  const meds=D.meds.length?D.meds.map(m=>`${m.name} ${m.dose||''} (${m.freq})`).join('<br>'):'None recorded';
  const appts=D.appts.filter(a=>new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00')>=new Date()).slice(0,4).map(a=>`${fmtDate(a.date)} — ${a.name}`).join('<br>')||'None upcoming';
  const lv=D.health[0];
  el.innerHTML=`<strong>Patient:</strong> ${D.settings.name||'Not set'}<br><strong>Doctor:</strong> ${D.settings.doc||'Not set'}<br><strong>Phone:</strong> ${D.settings.phone||'Not set'}<br><br><strong>Medications (${D.meds.length}):</strong><br>${meds}<br><br><strong>Latest Vitals:</strong> ${lv?`BP: ${lv.bp||'—'}, HR: ${lv.hr||'—'} bpm`:'Not recorded'}<br><br><strong>Upcoming Appointments:</strong><br>${appts}`;
}
function printHealthSummary(){
  const today=new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US',{weekday:'long',year:'numeric',month:'long',day:'numeric'});
  const meds=D.meds.map(m=>`  • ${m.name} ${m.dose||''} — ${m.freq}${m.time?' at '+m.time:''}${m.doctor?' (Dr. '+m.doctor+')':''}`).join('\n')||'  None recorded';
  const appts=D.appts.filter(a=>new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00')>=new Date()).map(a=>`  • ${fmtDate(a.date)} — ${a.name}${a.type?' ('+a.type+')':''}${a.loc?'\n    📍 '+a.loc:''}`).join('\n')||'  None upcoming';
  const vitals=D.health.slice(0,14).map(h=>`  ${fmtDate(h.date)} — BP: ${h.bp||'—'}, HR: ${h.hr||'—'} bpm, Wt: ${h.wt||'—'} lbs`).join('\n')||'  No entries';
  const syms=D.symptoms.slice(0,10).map(s=>`  ${new Date(s.dt).toLocaleDateString()} — ${s.symptoms.join(', ')} (${s.severity})`).join('\n')||'  None logged';
  const contacts=D.contacts.map(c=>`  ${c.name} (${c.type}): ${c.phone}`).join('\n')||'  None added';
  const lv=D.health[0];
  const w=window.open('','_blank');w.document.write(`<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><title>Health Summary</title><style>body{font-family:Georgia,serif;max-width:780px;margin:40px auto;color:#1E293B;font-size:14px;line-height:1.8}h1{font-size:1.8rem;color:#0F766E;border-bottom:3px solid #0F766E;padding-bottom:10px}h2{font-size:1.1rem;color:#475569;margin-top:28px;border-bottom:1px solid #E2D9CC;padding-bottom:4px}pre{white-space:pre-wrap;font-family:Georgia,serif;font-size:13px;padding-left:8px}.hg{display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:16px}.footer{margin-top:40px;font-size:11px;color:#94A3B8;border-top:1px solid #E2D9CC;padding-top:12px;text-align:center}@media print{body{margin:10px 20px}}

// AI Trend Analysis
async function runTrendAnalysis(){
  if(D.health.length<3){toast('Need at least 3 health log entries','var(--amber)');return;}
  const loading=document.getElementById('trend-loading'),results=document.getElementById('trend-results');
  loading.style.display='block';results.innerHTML='';
  const prog=document.getElementById('trend-progress');prog.style.width='0%';setTimeout(()=>prog.style.width='60%',100);
  const vitals=D.health.slice(0,14).map(h=>`${h.date}: BP ${h.bp||'?'}, HR ${h.hr||'?'} bpm, Wt ${h.wt||'?'} lbs, Sugar ${h.bs||'?'} mg/dL, Feel ${h.feel||'?'}/5`).join('\n');
  const meds=D.meds.map(m=>m.name+' '+m.dose).join(', ')||'none';
  const symptoms=D.symptoms.slice(0,10).map(s=>s.symptoms.join(', ')+' ('+s.severity+')').join('; ')||'none';
  const today=new Date().toDateString();const done=D.meds.filter(m=>D.medChecks[m.id+'_'+today]).length;
  try{
    prog.style.width='80%';
    const data=await apiFetch({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:1200,messages:[{role:'user',content:`You are a caring health assistant analyzing a senior patient's data. Use plain English.\n\nMedications: ${meds}\nMeds taken today: ${done}/${D.meds.length}\nVitals (newest first):\n${vitals}\nSymptoms: ${symptoms}\n\nAnalyze and respond in exactly this format:\n\n## 📊 Overall Health Snapshot\n[2-3 sentence summary]\n\n## 📈 Trends I Notice\n[3-5 specific observations]\n\n## ⚠️ Worth Mentioning to Your Doctor\n[2-4 specific things]\n\n## ✅ What You're Doing Well\n[2-3 positive observations]\n\n## 💡 Simple Suggestions\n[2-3 easy suggestions]\n\nBe warm, specific, use actual numbers. Never diagnose — always recommend consulting their doctor.`}]});
    prog.style.width='100%';const text=data.content?.[0]?.text||'Unable to analyze right now.';
    loading.style.display='none';
    const sections=text.split(/\n## /).filter(Boolean);
    const borders=['var(--teal-mid)','#C7D2FE','#FCD34D','#86EFAC','var(--teal-mid)'];
    results.innerHTML=sections.map((sec,i)=>{const lines=sec.split('\n');const title=lines[0].replace(/^## /,'');const body=lines.slice(1).join('\n').trim();return`<div class="card" style="margin-bottom:16px;border-left:4px solid ${borders[i%borders.length]}"><div class="card-title" style="font-size:1rem">${title}</div><div style="font-size:.92rem;line-height:1.8;color:var(--slate-mid);white-space:pre-wrap">${body}</div></div>`;}).join('')+`<div style="text-align:center;margin-top:8px"><button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="runTrendAnalysis()">🔄 Re-analyze</button><p style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--slate-light);margin-top:10px">Based on your last ${Math.min(D.health.length,14)} health entries. Always consult your doctor for medical advice.</p></div>`;
  }catch(e){loading.style.display='none';if(e.message!=='NO_KEY'&&e.message!=='INVALID_KEY')results.innerHTML='<div class="card" style="color:var(--rose)">Unable to connect. Please check your API key in Settings.</div>';}
}

// Medications
// ── Medication add / edit ──────────────────────────────────────
let _editMedId = null; // null = adding new, number = editing existing

function addMed(){
  _editMedId = null;
  document.getElementById('med-modal-title').textContent = '💊 Add Medication';
  document.getElementById('med-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Save';
  clearInputs(['m-name','m-dose','m-time','m-refill','m-doctor','m-notes']);
  document.getElementById('m-freq').value = 'Once daily';
  openModal('med-modal');
}

function editMed(id){
  const m = D.meds.find(x => x.id === id);
  if(!m) return;
  _editMedId = id;
  document.getElementById('med-modal-title').textContent = '✏️ Edit Medication';
  document.getElementById('med-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Update';
  document.getElementById('m-name').value    = m.name  || '';
  document.getElementById('m-dose').value    = m.dose  || '';
  document.getElementById('m-freq').value    = m.freq  || 'Once daily';
  document.getElementById('m-time').value    = m.time  || '';
  document.getElementById('m-refill').value  = m.refill|| '';
  document.getElementById('m-doctor').value  = m.doctor|| '';
  document.getElementById('m-notes').value   = m.notes || '';
  openModal('med-modal');
}

function medModalSave(){
  const name = document.getElementById('m-name').value.trim();
  if(!name){ toast('Please enter a medication name', 'var(--amber)'); return; }
  const fields = {
    name, dose: document.getElementById('m-dose').value,
    freq: document.getElementById('m-freq').value,
    time: document.getElementById('m-time').value,
    refill: document.getElementById('m-refill').value,
    doctor: document.getElementById('m-doctor').value,
    notes: document.getElementById('m-notes').value
  };
  if(_editMedId !== null){
    // Update existing
    const idx = D.meds.findIndex(m => m.id === _editMedId);
    if(idx !== -1) D.meds[idx] = { ...D.meds[idx], ...fields };
    toast('✅ Medication updated!', 'var(--sage)');
  } else {
    // Add new
    D.meds.push({ id: Date.now(), ...fields });
    toast('✅ Medication saved!', 'var(--sage)');
  }
  save();
  closeModal('med-modal');
  clearInputs(['m-name','m-dose','m-time','m-refill','m-doctor','m-notes']);
  _editMedId = null;
  renderAll();
}

function medModalCancel(){
  _editMedId = null;
  closeModal('med-modal');
}
function toggleMedCheck(key){if(caregiverMode)return;D.medChecks[key]=!D.medChecks[key];save();renderDashMeds();renderMedsChecklist();updateDashStats();}
function renderDashMeds(){
  const list=document.getElementById('d-med-list');if(!D.meds.length){list.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><div class="ei">💊</div><p>No medications yet.</p></div>';return;}
  const today=new Date().toDateString();let done=0;
  list.innerHTML=D.meds.map(m=>{const key=m.id+'_'+today;const chk=!!D.medChecks[key];if(chk)done++;return`<div class="med-row"><div class="check-box ${chk?'done':''}" onclick="toggleMedCheck('${key}')">${chk?'✓':''}</div><div style="flex:1"><div style="font-weight:600;${chk?'text-decoration:line-through;color:var(--slate-light)':''}">${m.name}</div><div style="font-size:.83rem;color:var(--slate-light)">${m.dose||''}${m.dose&&m.freq?' · ':''}${m.freq||''}</div></div>${m.time?`<div style="font-size:.82rem;font-weight:600;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:8px;background:var(--teal-pale);color:var(--teal)">${m.time}</div>`:''}</div>`;}).join('');
  document.getElementById('d-meds').textContent=done+'/'+D.meds.length;
  document.getElementById('d-med-prog').style.width=(D.meds.length?Math.round(done/D.meds.length*100):0)+'%';
}
function renderMedsChecklist(){
  const list=document.getElementById('meds-checklist');if(!D.meds.length){list.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><div class="ei">💊</div><p>Add medications to start tracking.</p></div>';return;}
  const today=new Date().toDateString();
  list.innerHTML=D.meds.map(m=>{const key=m.id+'_'+today;const chk=!!D.medChecks[key];return`<div class="med-row"><div class="check-box ${chk?'done':''}" onclick="toggleMedCheck('${key}')">${chk?'✓':''}</div><div style="flex:1"><div style="font-weight:600;${chk?'text-decoration:line-through;color:var(--slate-light)':''}">${m.name}</div><div style="font-size:.83rem;color:var(--slate-light)">${[m.dose,m.freq,m.doctor].filter(Boolean).join(' · ')}</div>${m.notes?`<div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--slate-light);margin-top:2px">📝 ${m.notes}</div>`:''}</div>${m.time?`<div style="font-size:.82rem;font-weight:600;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:8px;background:var(--teal-pale);color:var(--teal)">${m.time}</div>`:''}</div>`;}).join('');
}
function renderMedsCards(){
  const grid=document.getElementById('meds-cards');
  if(!D.meds.length){grid.innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--slate-light)">No medications added yet.</p>';return;}
  grid.innerHTML=D.meds.map(m=>{
    const rs=m.refill&&(new Date(m.refill+'T00:00:00')-new Date())<7*86400000;
    const inner=`<div class="card sw-inner" style="margin-bottom:0"><div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start"><div style="font-size:1.4rem">💊</div>${caregiverMode?'':`<div style="display:flex;gap:6px"><button onclick="editMed(${m.id})" class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm">✏️ Edit</button><button onclick="deleteMed(${m.id})" class="btn btn-danger btn-sm">✕</button></div>`}</div><div style="font-weight:700;font-size:1rem;margin-top:6px">${m.name}</div><div style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-light);margin-top:3px">${m.dose||''} · ${m.freq}</div>${m.doctor?`<div style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--slate-light);margin-top:2px">Dr: ${m.doctor}</div>`:''}<div style="margin-top:10px;display:flex;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap">${m.time?`<span style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:600;padding:2px 9px;border-radius:8px;background:var(--teal-pale);color:var(--teal)">⏰ ${m.time}</span>`:''}${m.refill?`<span style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:600;padding:2px 9px;border-radius:8px;background:${rs?'var(--rose-pale)':'var(--amber-pale)'};color:${rs?'var(--rose)':'var(--amber)'}">📅 ${m.refill}</span>`:''}</div></div>`;
    return caregiverMode?inner:`<div class="sw-wrap">${inner}<div class="sw-del" onclick="deleteMed(${m.id})"><span>🗑️</span>Delete</div></div>`;
  }).join('');
  if(!caregiverMode) initSwipe('.sw-wrap');
}

function deleteMed(id){if(!confirm('Remove?'))return;D.meds=D.meds.filter(m=>m.id!==id);save();renderAll();}

let _editApptId = null;

function addAppt(){
  _editApptId = null;
  document.getElementById('appt-modal-title').textContent = '📅 Add Appointment';
  document.getElementById('appt-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Save';
  clearInputs(['a-name','a-type','a-time','a-loc','a-phone','a-notes']);
  document.getElementById('a-date').value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  document.getElementById('a-transport').value = '';
  openModal('appt-modal');
}

function editAppt(id){
  const a = D.appts.find(x => x.id === id);
  if(!a) return;
  _editApptId = id;
  document.getElementById('appt-modal-title').textContent = '✏️ Edit Appointment';
  document.getElementById('appt-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Update';
  document.getElementById('a-name').value      = a.name      || '';
  document.getElementById('a-type').value      = a.type      || '';
  document.getElementById('a-date').value      = a.date      || '';
  document.getElementById('a-time').value      = a.time      || '';
  document.getElementById('a-loc').value       = a.loc       || '';
  document.getElementById('a-phone').value     = a.phone     || '';
  document.getElementById('a-notes').value     = a.notes     || '';
  document.getElementById('a-transport').value = a.transport || '';
  openModal('appt-modal');
}

function apptModalSave(){
  const name = document.getElementById('a-name').value.trim();
  const date = document.getElementById('a-date').value;
  if(!name || !date){ toast('Please fill in doctor name and date', 'var(--amber)'); return; }
  const fields = {
    name, date,
    type:      document.getElementById('a-type').value,
    time:      document.getElementById('a-time').value,
    loc:       document.getElementById('a-loc').value,
    phone:     document.getElementById('a-phone').value,
    notes:     document.getElementById('a-notes').value,
    transport: document.getElementById('a-transport').value
  };
  if(_editApptId !== null){
    const idx = D.appts.findIndex(a => a.id === _editApptId);
    if(idx !== -1) D.appts[idx] = { ...D.appts[idx], ...fields };
    toast('✅ Appointment updated!', 'var(--sage)');
  } else {
    D.appts.push({ id: Date.now(), ...fields });
    toast('✅ Appointment saved!', 'var(--sage)');
  }
  D.appts.sort((a,b) => new Date(a.date) - new Date(b.date));
  save();
  closeModal('appt-modal');
  clearInputs(['a-name','a-type','a-date','a-time','a-loc','a-phone','a-notes']);
  _editApptId = null;
  renderAll();
}

function apptModalCancel(){
  _editApptId = null;
  closeModal('appt-modal');
}
function renderAppts(cId,limit=999){
  const el=document.getElementById(cId);if(!el)return;
  const today=new Date().toDateString();const upcoming=D.appts.filter(a=>new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00')>=new Date(today)).slice(0,limit);
  document.getElementById('d-appts').textContent=upcoming.length;
  if(!upcoming.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><div class="ei">📅</div><p>No upcoming appointments.</p></div>';return;}
  el.innerHTML=upcoming.map(a=>{const d=new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00');return`<div class="appt-row"><div class="date-block"><div class="mo">${d.toLocaleString('en-US',{month:'short'})}</div><div class="dy">${d.getDate()}</div></div><div style="flex:1"><div style="font-weight:700">${a.name}</div><div style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-light)">${[a.type,a.loc,a.time?'⏰ '+fmtTime(a.time):''].filter(Boolean).join(' · ')}</div>${a.notes?`<div style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--slate-light);margin-top:3px">📝 ${a.notes}</div>`:''}${a.transport?`<div style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--indigo);margin-top:2px">🚗 ${a.transport}</div>`:''}</div>${cId==='appts-full'&&!caregiverMode?`<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px"><button onclick="editAppt(${a.id})" class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm">✏️ Edit</button><button onclick="deleteAppt(${a.id})" class="btn btn-danger btn-sm">✕ Remove</button></div>`:''}</div>`;}).join('');
}
function deleteAppt(id){if(!confirm('Remove?'))return;D.appts=D.appts.filter(a=>a.id!==id);save();renderAll();}

function addHealth(){
  _editHealthId = null;
  document.getElementById('health-modal-title').textContent = '❤️ Log Health Entry';
  document.getElementById('health-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Save';
  clearInputs(['h-bp','h-hr','h-wt','h-bs','h-temp','h-o2','h-notes']);
  document.getElementById('h-feel').value = '';
  document.getElementById('h-date').value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  openModal('health-modal');
}

function editHealth(id){
  const h = D.health.find(x => x.id === id);
  if(!h) return;
  _editHealthId = id;
  document.getElementById('health-modal-title').textContent = '✏️ Edit Health Entry';
  document.getElementById('health-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Update';
  document.getElementById('h-date').value  = h.date  || '';
  document.getElementById('h-bp').value    = h.bp    || '';
  document.getElementById('h-hr').value    = h.hr    || '';
  document.getElementById('h-wt').value    = h.wt    || '';
  document.getElementById('h-bs').value    = h.bs    || '';
  document.getElementById('h-temp').value  = h.temp  || '';
  document.getElementById('h-o2').value    = h.o2    || '';
  document.getElementById('h-feel').value  = h.feel  || '';
  document.getElementById('h-notes').value = h.notes || '';
  openModal('health-modal');

function healthModalSave(){
  const fields = {
    date:  document.getElementById('h-date').value  || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],
    bp:    document.getElementById('h-bp').value,
    hr:    document.getElementById('h-hr').value,
    wt:    document.getElementById('h-wt').value,
    bs:    document.getElementById('h-bs').value,
    temp:  document.getElementById('h-temp').value,
    o2:    document.getElementById('h-o2').value,
    feel:  document.getElementById('h-feel').value,
    notes: document.getElementById('h-notes').value
  };
  if(_editHealthId !== null){
    const idx = D.health.findIndex(h => h.id === _editHealthId);
    if(idx !== -1) D.health[idx] = { ...D.health[idx], ...fields };
    toast('✅ Health entry updated!', 'var(--sage)');
  } else {
    D.health.push({ id: Date.now(), ...fields });
    toast('✅ Logged!', 'var(--sage)');
  }
  D.health.sort((a,b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date));
  save(); document.getElementById('health-modal')?.querySelector('.modal')?.classList.remove('dirty'); closeModal('health-modal', true);
  clearInputs(['h-bp','h-hr','h-wt','h-bs','h-temp','h-o2','h-notes']);
  document.getElementById('h-feel').value = '';
  _editHealthId = null;
  renderAll();
  checkBpAlert();
}

function healthModalCancel(){ _editHealthId = null; closeModal('health-modal'); }
function renderHealth(){
  const el=document.getElementById('health-entries');document.getElementById('d-logs').textContent=D.health.length;
  if(!D.health.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><div class="ei">❤️</div><p>Start logging vitals to track trends.</p></div>';updateHealthScore();return;}
  const fe={5:'😄',4:'🙂',3:'😐',2:'😕',1:'😞'};
  el.innerHTML=D.health.map(h=>`<div class="log-entry"><div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center"><strong>${fmtDate(h.date)} ${h.feel?fe[h.feel]||'':''}</strong>${caregiverMode?'':`<div style="display:flex;gap:6px"><button onclick="editHealth(${h.id})" class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm">✏️ Edit</button><button onclick="deleteHealth(${h.id})" class="btn btn-danger btn-sm">✕</button></div>`}</div><div class="vital-grid">${h.bp?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${h.bp}</div><div class="vital-name">Blood Pressure</div></div>`:''}${h.hr?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${h.hr}</div><div class="vital-name">Heart Rate</div></div>`:''}${h.wt?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${h.wt}</div><div class="vital-name">Weight (lbs)</div></div>`:''}${h.bs?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${h.bs}</div><div class="vital-name">Blood Sugar</div></div>`:''}${h.temp?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${h.temp}°</div><div class="vital-name">Temp</div></div>`:''}${h.o2?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${h.o2}%</div><div class="vital-name">Oxygen</div></div>`:''}</div>${h.notes?`<div style="margin-top:10px;font-size:.85rem;padding:10px;background:var(--cream);border-radius:8px">📝 ${h.notes}</div>`:''}</div>`).join('');
  updateHealthScore();
}
function deleteHealth(id){D.health=D.health.filter(h=>h.id!==id);save();renderAll();}
function updateHealthScore(){
  const el=document.getElementById('health-score'),desc=document.getElementById('health-score-desc'),vitals=document.getElementById('dash-latest-vitals');
  if(!D.health.length){if(el)el.textContent='--';if(desc)desc.textContent='Log vitals to get your score.';if(vitals)vitals.innerHTML='';return;}
  let score=60;const lv=D.health[0];if(lv.feel)score+=parseInt(lv.feel)*4;
  if(D.meds.length){const today=new Date().toDateString();const done=D.meds.filter(m=>D.medChecks[m.id+'_'+today]).length;score+=Math.round(done/D.meds.length*10);}
  score=Math.min(100,Math.max(30,score));
  if(el)el.textContent=score;if(desc)desc.textContent=`${score>=80?'Excellent':score>=60?'Good':'Keep going'} — keep up with medications and daily logs!`;
  if(vitals&&lv)vitals.innerHTML=`<div class="vital-grid" style="margin-top:0">${lv.bp?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${lv.bp}</div><div class="vital-name">BP</div></div>`:''}${lv.hr?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${lv.hr}</div><div class="vital-name">HR</div></div>`:''}${lv.wt?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${lv.wt}</div><div class="vital-name">Weight</div></div>`:''}${lv.bs?`<div class="vital-box"><div class="vital-val">${lv.bs}</div><div class="vital-name">Sugar</div></div>`:''}</div>`;
}

// Symptoms
let selSev='';
function toggleSymptom(el){el.classList.toggle('selected');}
function selectSev(el,v){document.querySelectorAll('.sev-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('sel'));el.classList.add('sel');selSev=v;}
// ── Symptom add / edit ────────────────────────────────
let _editSymId = null;

function addSymptom(){
  _editSymId = null;
  document.getElementById('symptom-modal-title').textContent = '🌡️ Log Symptom';
  document.getElementById('symptom-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Log';
  document.querySelectorAll('#symptom-chips .symptom-chip').forEach(c=>c.classList.remove('selected'));
  clearInputs(['sy-other','sy-notes']);
  document.querySelectorAll('.sev-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('sel'));
  selSev='';
  const n=new Date(); n.setMinutes(0,0,0);
  document.getElementById('sy-dt').value = n.toISOString().slice(0,16);
  openModal('symptom-modal');
}

function editSym(id){
  const s = D.symptoms.find(x => x.id === id);
  if(!s) return;
  _editSymId = id;
  document.getElementById('symptom-modal-title').textContent = '✏️ Edit Symptom';
  document.getElementById('symptom-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Update';
  // Reset then pre-select chips
  document.querySelectorAll('#symptom-chips .symptom-chip').forEach(c=>{
    c.classList.toggle('selected', s.symptoms.includes(c.textContent.trim()));
  });
  document.getElementById('sy-dt').value    = s.dt ? s.dt.slice(0,16) : '';
  document.getElementById('sy-other').value = '';
  document.getElementById('sy-notes').value = s.notes || '';
  document.querySelectorAll('.sev-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('sel'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.sev-btn').forEach(b=>{
    if(b.getAttribute('onclick')&&b.getAttribute('onclick').includes("'"+s.severity+"'")) b.classList.add('sel');
  });
  selSev = s.severity || 'mild';
  openModal('symptom-modal');
}

function symModalSave(){
  const chips=[...document.querySelectorAll('#symptom-chips .symptom-chip.selected')].map(c=>c.textContent.trim());
  const other=document.getElementById('sy-other').value.trim();
  const all=[...chips,...(other?other.split(',').map(s=>s.trim()):[])];
  if(!all.length){toast('Please select at least one symptom','var(--amber)');return;}
  const fields = {
    dt:       document.getElementById('sy-dt').value || new Date().toISOString(),
    symptoms: all,
    severity: selSev || 'mild',
    notes:    document.getElementById('sy-notes').value
  };
  if(_editSymId !== null){
    const idx = D.symptoms.findIndex(s => s.id === _editSymId);
    if(idx !== -1) D.symptoms[idx] = { ...D.symptoms[idx], ...fields };
    toast('✅ Symptom updated!','var(--sage)');
  } else {
    D.symptoms.push({ id: Date.now(), ...fields });
    toast('✅ Symptom logged!','var(--sage)');
  }
  D.symptoms.sort((a,b)=>new Date(b.dt)-new Date(a.dt));
  save(); document.getElementById('symptom-modal')?.querySelector('.modal')?.classList.remove('dirty'); closeModal('symptom-modal', true);
  document.querySelectorAll('#symptom-chips .symptom-chip').forEach(c=>c.classList.remove('selected'));
  clearInputs(['sy-other','sy-notes']);
  document.querySelectorAll('.sev-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('sel'));
  selSev=''; _editSymId=null; renderAll();
}

function symModalCancel(){ _editSymId=null; closeModal('symptom-modal'); }
function renderSymptoms(){
  const list=document.getElementById('symptom-log'),sum=document.getElementById('symptom-summary');
  if(!D.symptoms.length){list.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><div class="ei">🌡️</div><p>No symptoms logged yet.</p></div>';sum.innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--slate-light)">Log symptoms to see patterns.</p>';return;}
  const sc={mild:['var(--sage-pale)','var(--sage)'],moderate:['var(--amber-pale)','var(--amber)'],severe:['var(--rose-pale)','var(--rose)']};
  list.innerHTML=D.symptoms.map(s=>{const[bg,fg]=sc[s.severity]||sc.mild;const dt=new Date(s.dt);return`<div class="log-entry" style="margin-bottom:10px"><div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div><strong>${dt.toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric'})}</strong><span style="margin-left:8px;font-size:.78rem;font-weight:700;padding:2px 10px;border-radius:8px;background:${bg};color:${fg}">${s.severity}</span></div>${caregiverMode?'':`<div style="display:flex;gap:6px"><button onclick="editSym(${s.id})" class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm">✏️ Edit</button><button onclick="deleteSym(${s.id})" class="btn btn-danger btn-sm">✕</button></div>`}</div><div style="margin-top:8px;display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:5px">${s.symptoms.map(sy=>`<span style="font-size:.82rem;padding:3px 10px;background:var(--cream);border:1.5px solid var(--border);border-radius:12px">${sy}</span>`).join('')}</div>${s.notes?`<div style="font-size:.83rem;color:var(--slate-mid);margin-top:8px">📝 ${s.notes}</div>`:''}</div>`;}).join('');
  const counts={};D.symptoms.forEach(s=>s.symptoms.forEach(sy=>{counts[sy]=(counts[sy]||0)+1;}));
  const sorted=Object.entries(counts).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).slice(0,5);
  sum.innerHTML=`<div style="font-weight:600;margin-bottom:10px">Most frequent:</div>${sorted.map(([s,c])=>`<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:.88rem;margin-bottom:6px"><span>${s}</span><span style="font-weight:700;color:var(--teal)">${c}x</span></div><div class="progress-wrap" style="margin-bottom:10px"><div class="progress-fill" style="width:${Math.round(c/D.symptoms.length*100)}%;background:var(--teal-mid)"></div></div>`).join('')}`;
}
function deleteSym(id){D.symptoms=D.symptoms.filter(s=>s.id!==id);save();renderAll();}
function exportSymptoms(){if(!D.symptoms.length){toast('No symptoms to export');return;}const lines=['SYMPTOM LOG — Tended','Generated: '+new Date().toLocaleDateString(),'','Date | Symptoms | Severity | Notes'];D.symptoms.forEach(s=>lines.push(`${new Date(s.dt).toLocaleDateString()} | ${s.symptoms.join(', ')} | ${s.severity} | ${s.notes||''}`));const blob=new Blob([lines.join('\n')],{type:'text/plain'});const a=document.createElement('a');a.href=URL.createObjectURL(blob);a.download='symptom-log.txt';a.click();toast('✅ Exported!','var(--sage)');}

// Insurance
function addClaim(){const desc=document.getElementById('cl-desc').value.trim();if(!desc){toast('Please enter a description');return;}D.claims.push({id:Date.now(),desc,date:document.getElementById('cl-date').value,amt:document.getElementById('cl-amt').value,prov:document.getElementById('cl-prov').value,num:document.getElementById('cl-num').value,status:document.getElementById('cl-status').value,paid:document.getElementById('cl-paid').value});save();closeModal('claim-modal');clearInputs(['cl-desc','cl-date','cl-amt','cl-prov','cl-num','cl-paid']);renderAll();toast('✅ Claim saved!','var(--sage)');}
function renderClaims(){
  const el=document.getElementById('claims-full'),stats=document.getElementById('insurance-stats');
  const pending=D.claims.filter(c=>c.status==='pending'||c.status==='review').length;
  document.getElementById('d-claims').textContent=pending;
  const nb=document.getElementById('nb-claims');if(pending>0){nb.textContent=pending;nb.style.display='inline';}else nb.style.display='none';
  const total=D.claims.reduce((s,c)=>s+(parseFloat(c.amt)||0),0),paid=D.claims.reduce((s,c)=>s+(parseFloat(c.paid)||0),0);
  stats.innerHTML=`<div class="card" style="flex:1;min-width:120px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:800">${D.claims.length}</div><div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--slate-light)">Total</div></div><div class="card" style="flex:1;min-width:120px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--amber)">${pending}</div><div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--slate-light)">Pending</div></div><div class="card" style="flex:1;min-width:120px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:800">$${total.toFixed(0)}</div><div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--slate-light)">Billed</div></div><div class="card" style="flex:1;min-width:120px;text-align:center"><div style="font-size:1.4rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--sage)">$${paid.toFixed(0)}</div><div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--slate-light)">Paid</div></div>`;
  if(!D.claims.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><div class="ei">📋</div><p>No claims yet.</p></div>';return;}
  const labels={approved:'Approved ✓',pending:'Pending…',review:'Under Review',denied:'Denied'};
  el.innerHTML=D.claims.map(c=>`<div class="claim-row"><div class="status-dot ${c.status}"></div><div style="flex:1"><strong>${c.desc}</strong><div style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--slate-light)">${[c.prov,c.date,c.num?'#'+c.num:''].filter(Boolean).join(' · ')}</div><div style="font-size:.83rem;font-weight:600;color:${c.status==='approved'?'var(--sage)':c.status==='denied'?'var(--rose)':'var(--amber)'}">${labels[c.status]||c.status}</div></div><div style="text-align:right">${c.amt?`<div style="font-weight:700">$${parseFloat(c.amt).toFixed(2)}</div>`:''}${c.paid?`<div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--sage)">Paid: $${parseFloat(c.paid).toFixed(2)}</div>`:''}</div>${caregiverMode?'':`<button onclick="deleteClaim(${c.id})" class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" style="margin-left:10px">✕</button>`}</div>`).join('');
}
function deleteClaim(id){D.claims=D.claims.filter(c=>c.id!==id);save();renderAll();}
