// Drug Interaction Checker
function renderMyMedsList(){
  const el=document.getElementById('my-meds-interaction-list');if(!el)return;
  if(!D.meds.length){el.innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:.9rem">No medications saved yet. Add medications first.</p>';return;}
  el.innerHTML=`<p style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-mid);margin-bottom:10px">Your ${D.meds.length} saved medication${D.meds.length>1?'s':''}: <strong>${D.meds.map(m=>m.name).join(', ')}</strong></p>`;
  // Pre-fill datalists
  const listA=document.getElementById('drug-a-list');const listB=document.getElementById('drug-b-list');
  if(listA)listA.innerHTML=D.meds.map(m=>`<option value="${m.name}">`).join('');
  if(listB)listB.innerHTML=D.meds.map(m=>`<option value="${m.name}">`).join('');
}

async function checkTwoMeds(){
  const a=document.getElementById('drug-a').value.trim();const b=document.getElementById('drug-b').value.trim();
  if(!a||!b){toast('Please enter both medications','var(--amber)');return;}
  const result=document.getElementById('two-med-result');
  result.innerHTML=`<div class="scam-alert" style="background:var(--indigo-pale);border-color:#C7D2FE">⚗️ Checking interaction between <strong>${a}</strong> and <strong>${b}</strong>…</div>`;
  try{
    const data=await apiFetch({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:700,messages:[{role:'user',content:`You are a pharmacist assistant helping a senior patient check for drug interactions. Provide clear, plain-English information.

Check the interaction between: "${a}" and "${b}"

Respond in exactly this format:

SEVERITY: [NONE / MINOR / MODERATE / MAJOR]
SUMMARY: [1-2 sentence plain-English summary]
DETAILS: [2-4 sentences explaining what happens and why it matters]
ACTION: [What the patient should do — e.g. "Ask your doctor", "Monitor for symptoms", "Generally safe but tell your pharmacist", etc.]
SYMPTOMS_TO_WATCH: [List any symptoms to watch for, or "None" if no interaction]

Be warm and reassuring. If there is no significant interaction, say so clearly. Never tell them to stop taking medications — always refer to their doctor or pharmacist.`}]});
    const text=data.content?.[0]?.text||'Unable to check right now.';
    renderInteractionResult(text,a,b,'two-med-result');
  }catch(e){if(e.message!=='NO_KEY'&&e.message!=='INVALID_KEY')result.innerHTML='<div class="scam-alert red">Unable to connect. Please check your API key in Settings.</div>';}
}

async function checkMyMeds(){
  if(D.meds.length<2){toast('You need at least 2 medications saved to check interactions','var(--amber)');return;}
  const result=document.getElementById('all-meds-result');
  result.innerHTML=`<div class="scam-alert" style="background:var(--indigo-pale);border-color:#C7D2FE">⚗️ Checking all ${D.meds.length} medications for interactions…<div style="margin-top:8px;height:4px;background:rgba(0,0,0,.1);border-radius:4px;overflow:hidden"><div style="height:100%;background:var(--indigo);border-radius:4px;width:0%;transition:width 2s ease" id="int-progress"></div></div></div>`;
  setTimeout(()=>{const p=document.getElementById('int-progress');if(p)p.style.width='70%';},100);
  const medList=D.meds.map(m=>`${m.name}${m.dose?' '+m.dose:''}`).join(', ');
  try{
    const data=await apiFetch({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:1400,messages:[{role:'user',content:`You are a pharmacist assistant helping a senior patient review all their medications for interactions. Be clear and plain-English.

Patient's full medication list: ${medList}

Check ALL significant pairwise interactions. For each notable interaction found, use this format:

## [Drug A] + [Drug B]
SEVERITY: [MINOR / MODERATE / MAJOR]
ISSUE: [1 sentence what the problem is]
ACTION: [What to do]

If there are no significant interactions, say so clearly and reassuringly.

At the end, add a ## OVERALL SUMMARY section with 2-3 sentences about the overall safety of this medication combination and the most important thing to discuss with their doctor or pharmacist.

Be warm and thorough. Always refer to their doctor/pharmacist for final guidance.`}]});
    const p=document.getElementById('int-progress');if(p)p.style.width='100%';
    setTimeout(()=>{
      const text=data.content?.[0]?.text||'Unable to check right now.';
      renderAllMedsResult(text);
    },300);
  }catch(e){if(e.message!=='NO_KEY'&&e.message!=='INVALID_KEY')result.innerHTML='<div class="scam-alert red">Unable to connect. Please check your API key in Settings.</div>';}
}

function renderInteractionResult(text,drugA,drugB,containerId){
  const el=document.getElementById(containerId);if(!el)return;
  const sev=text.match(/SEVERITY:\s*(\w+)/i)?.[1]?.toUpperCase()||'UNKNOWN';
  const summary=text.match(/SUMMARY:\s*(.+?)(?=\nDETAILS:|$)/is)?.[1]?.trim()||'';
  const details=text.match(/DETAILS:\s*(.+?)(?=\nACTION:|$)/is)?.[1]?.trim()||'';
  const action=text.match(/ACTION:\s*(.+?)(?=\nSYMPTOMS|$)/is)?.[1]?.trim()||'';
  const symptoms=text.match(/SYMPTOMS_TO_WATCH:\s*(.+?)$/is)?.[1]?.trim()||'None';
  const configs={
    'NONE':{bg:'var(--sage-pale)',border:'#86EFAC',icon:'✅',label:'No Significant Interaction',color:'var(--sage)'},
    'MINOR':{bg:'var(--teal-pale)',border:'var(--teal-mid)',icon:'💙',label:'Minor Interaction',color:'var(--teal)'},
    'MODERATE':{bg:'var(--amber-pale)',border:'#FCD34D',icon:'⚠️',label:'Moderate Interaction',color:'var(--amber)'},
    'MAJOR':{bg:'var(--rose-pale)',border:'#FCA5A5',icon:'🚨',label:'Major Interaction — Talk to Your Doctor',color:'var(--rose)'},
    'UNKNOWN':{bg:'var(--indigo-pale)',border:'#C7D2FE',icon:'❓',label:'Interaction Unknown',color:'var(--indigo)'}
  };
  const cfg=configs[sev]||configs['UNKNOWN'];
  el.innerHTML=`<div style="background:${cfg.bg};border:1.5px solid ${cfg.border};border-radius:var(--r);padding:18px 20px">
    <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;margin-bottom:12px">
      <span style="font-size:1.4rem">${cfg.icon}</span>
      <div><div style="font-weight:700;font-size:1rem;color:${cfg.color}">${cfg.label}</div><div style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--slate-light);margin-top:2px">${drugA} + ${drugB}</div></div>
    </div>
    ${summary?`<div style="font-size:.92rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--slate);margin-bottom:8px">${summary}</div>`:''}
    ${details?`<div style="font-size:.88rem;color:var(--slate-mid);margin-bottom:10px;line-height:1.7">${details}</div>`:''}
    ${action?`<div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.6);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 14px;font-size:.88rem;margin-bottom:8px"><strong>What to do:</strong> ${action}</div>`:''}
    ${symptoms&&symptoms.toLowerCase()!=='none'?`<div style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-mid)"><strong>Watch for:</strong> ${symptoms}</div>`:''}
    <div style="margin-top:12px;font-size:.78rem;color:var(--slate-light)">⚕️ Always confirm with your doctor or pharmacist before making any medication changes.</div>
  </div>`;
}

function renderAllMedsResult(text){
  const el=document.getElementById('all-meds-result');if(!el)return;
  const sections=text.split(/\n## /).filter(Boolean);
  if(!sections.length){el.innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--slate-light)">No interactions found.</p>';return;}
  const sevColors={MAJOR:['var(--rose-pale)','#FCA5A5','🚨','var(--rose)'],MODERATE:['var(--amber-pale)','#FCD34D','⚠️','var(--amber)'],MINOR:['var(--teal-pale)','var(--teal-mid)','💙','var(--teal)']};
  let html='';
  sections.forEach(sec=>{
    const lines=sec.split('\n').filter(Boolean);
    const title=lines[0].replace(/^## /,'');
    const body=lines.slice(1).join('\n');
    if(title.includes('OVERALL SUMMARY')){
      html+=`<div class="card" style="margin-top:16px;border-left:4px solid var(--teal)"><div class="card-title" style="font-size:1rem">📋 Overall Summary</div><div style="font-size:.9rem;color:var(--slate-mid);line-height:1.7;white-space:pre-wrap">${body.trim()}</div></div>`;
    } else {
      const sev=(body.match(/SEVERITY:\s*(\w+)/i)?.[1]||'MINOR').toUpperCase();
      const issue=body.match(/ISSUE:\s*(.+?)(?=\nACTION:|$)/is)?.[1]?.trim()||'';
      const action=body.match(/ACTION:\s*(.+?)$/is)?.[1]?.trim()||'';
      const[bg,border,icon,color]=sevColors[sev]||sevColors.MINOR;
      html+=`<div style="background:${bg};border:1.5px solid ${border};border-radius:var(--r-sm);padding:14px 16px;margin-bottom:10px">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;margin-bottom:6px"><span>${icon}</span><strong style="color:${color};font-size:.92rem">${title}</strong><span style="margin-left:auto;font-size:.75rem;font-weight:700;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:8px;background:${bg};color:${color};border:1px solid ${border}">${sev}</span></div>
        ${issue?`<div style="font-size:.88rem;color:var(--slate-mid);margin-bottom:6px">${issue}</div>`:''}
        ${action?`<div style="font-size:.85rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--slate)">→ ${action}</div>`:''}
      </div>`;
    }
  });
  if(!html.includes('card')){
    el.innerHTML=`<div class="scam-alert green" style="margin-bottom:0"><strong>✅ No significant interactions found</strong><div style="font-size:.88rem;margin-top:6px">${text.replace(/##.*/g,'').trim()}</div></div>`;
  } else {
    el.innerHTML=html;
  }
}

// Scam
const scamTips=[{color:'red',icon:'📞',title:'Medicare Card Scam',desc:'Medicare will NEVER call asking for your card or SSN.'},{color:'amber',icon:'🎁',title:'Gift Card Scam',desc:'No government agency ever asks for payment in gift cards.'},{color:'amber',icon:'💻',title:'Tech Support Scam',desc:'Microsoft and Apple never call about your computer.'},{color:'amber',icon:'🏦',title:'Grandchild in Trouble',desc:'Call the grandchild directly to verify before sending money.'},{color:'amber',icon:'💰',title:'Lottery Scam',desc:'Never pay a fee to collect a "prize."'}];
function populateScamTips(){const list=document.getElementById('scam-tips-list');if(!list)return;list.innerHTML=scamTips.map(t=>`<div class="scam-alert ${t.color==='red'?'red':''}" style="margin-bottom:10px;${t.color==='amber'?'background:var(--amber-pale);border-color:#FCD34D':''}"><strong>${t.icon} ${t.title}</strong><div style="font-size:.85rem;margin-top:4px">${t.desc}</div></div>`).join('');}
async function checkScam(){
  const input=document.getElementById('scam-input').value.trim();if(!input){toast('Please describe the call or text');return;}
  const result=document.getElementById('scam-result');result.innerHTML='<div class="scam-alert" style="background:var(--indigo-pale);border-color:#C7D2FE">🤖 Analyzing…</div>';
  try{const data=await apiFetch({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:600,messages:[{role:'user',content:`Scam detection for seniors. Analyze:\n\n"${input}"\n\nRISK: [LOW/MEDIUM/HIGH]\nVERDICT: [1 sentence]\nRED FLAGS: [bullets or "None"]\nADVICE: [2-3 sentences]`}]});
    const text=data.content?.[0]?.text||'Unable to analyze.';const risk=text.includes('RISK: HIGH')?'high':text.includes('RISK: MEDIUM')?'medium':'low';
    const cols={high:['var(--rose-pale)','#FCA5A5','🚨 HIGH RISK'],medium:['var(--amber-pale)','#FCD34D','⚠️ POSSIBLE SCAM'],low:['var(--sage-pale)','#86EFAC','✅ LIKELY SAFE']};
    const[bg,border,label]=cols[risk];result.innerHTML=`<div class="scam-alert" style="background:${bg};border-color:${border}"><div style="font-size:1.1rem;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:8px">${label}</div><div style="font-size:.9rem;line-height:1.7;white-space:pre-wrap">${text.replace(/RISK:.*\n/,'')}</div></div>`;
  }catch(e){if(e.message!=='NO_KEY'&&e.message!=='INVALID_KEY')result.innerHTML='<div class="scam-alert red">Unable to connect. If something feels wrong, hang up and call a trusted family member.</div>';}
}

// Family & Contacts
const famAvatars=['👩','👨','👴','👵','🧑','👱'];
function addFamily(){const name=document.getElementById('f-name').value.trim();if(!name){toast('Please enter a name');return;}const al={all:['Medications','Appointments','Health Log'],appts:['Appointments'],emergency:['Emergency Contact']};const access=document.getElementById('f-access').value;D.family.push({id:Date.now(),name,rel:document.getElementById('f-rel').value,phone:document.getElementById('f-phone').value,email:document.getElementById('f-email').value,access,labels:al[access]});save();closeModal('family-modal');clearInputs(['f-name','f-phone','f-email']);renderAll();toast('✅ Added!','var(--sage)');}
function renderFamily(){
  const el=document.getElementById('family-list-area');
  if(!D.family.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><div class="ei">👨‍👩‍👧</div><p>Add family members to the loop.</p></div>';return;}
  el.innerHTML=D.family.map((f,i)=>`
    <div class="family-card">
      <div style="width:56px;height:56px;border-radius:50%;background:#${['DBEAFE','D1FAE5','FEF3C7','EDE9FE','FFE4E6'][i%5]};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:1.6rem;flex-shrink:0">${famAvatars[i%famAvatars.length]}</div>
      <div style="flex:1">
        <strong>${f.name}</strong>
        <div style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-light)">${f.rel}${f.phone?' · '+f.phone:''}</div>
        <div style="margin-top:7px;display:flex;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap">${f.labels.map(l=>`<span class="access-pill">👁 ${l}</span>`).join('')}</div>
      </div>
      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:7px;align-items:flex-end">
        ${f.phone?`<button class="call-btn btn-sm" onclick="toast('📞 Calling ${f.name}...')">📞 Call</button>`:''}
        <button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="removeFamily(${f.id})" style="white-space:nowrap">✕ Remove</button>
      </div>
    </div>`).join('');
}

function removeFamily(id){
  const f = D.family.find(m => m.id === id);
  if(!f) return;
  if(!confirm(`Remove ${f.name} from your Family Loop?`)) return;
  D.family = D.family.filter(m => m.id !== id);
  save(); renderFamily();
  toast(`${f.name} removed from Family Loop`, 'var(--slate)');
}
// ── Contact add / edit ───────────────────────────────────────
let _editContactId = null;

function addContact(){
  _editContactId = null;
  document.getElementById('contact-modal-title').textContent = '📞 Add Contact';
  document.getElementById('contact-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Save';
  clearInputs(['co-name','co-phone','co-addr','co-notes']);
  document.getElementById('co-type').value = 'Doctor';
  document.getElementById('co-onqr').checked = false;
  openModal('contact-modal');
}

function editContact(id){
  const c = D.contacts.find(x => x.id === id);
  if(!c) return;
  _editContactId = id;
  document.getElementById('contact-modal-title').textContent = '✏️ Edit Contact';
  document.getElementById('contact-modal-save-btn').textContent = 'Update';
  document.getElementById('co-name').value  = c.name  || '';
  document.getElementById('co-type').value  = c.type  || 'Doctor';
  document.getElementById('co-phone').value = c.phone || '';
  document.getElementById('co-addr').value  = c.addr  || '';
  document.getElementById('co-notes').value = c.notes || '';
  document.getElementById('co-onqr').checked = !!c.onQR;
  openModal('contact-modal');
}

function contactModalSave(){
  const name  = document.getElementById('co-name').value.trim();
  const phone = document.getElementById('co-phone').value.trim();
  if(!name || !phone){ toast('Please enter name and phone number', 'var(--amber)'); return; }
  const fields = {
    name, phone,
    type:  document.getElementById('co-type').value,
    addr:  document.getElementById('co-addr').value,
    notes: document.getElementById('co-notes').value,
    onQR:  document.getElementById('co-onqr').checked
  };
  if(_editContactId !== null){
    const idx = D.contacts.findIndex(c => c.id === _editContactId);
    if(idx !== -1) D.contacts[idx] = { ...D.contacts[idx], ...fields };
    toast('✅ Contact updated!', 'var(--sage)');
  } else {
    D.contacts.push({ id: Date.now(), ...fields });
    toast('✅ Contact saved!', 'var(--sage)');
  }
  save();
  closeModal('contact-modal');
  clearInputs(['co-name','co-phone','co-addr','co-notes']);
  _editContactId = null;
  renderAll();
}

function contactModalCancel(){
  _editContactId = null;
  closeModal('contact-modal');
}
function renderContacts(){
  const el=document.getElementById('contacts-area');const ti={Doctor:'🩺',Specialist:'👨‍⚕️',Pharmacy:'💊',Hospital:'🏥',Family:'👨‍👩‍👧',Neighbor:'🏠',Caregiver:'🤝',Other:'📞'};
  const custom=D.contacts.map((c,i)=>`<div class="contact-card"><div class="contact-avatar" style="background:#${['DBEAFE','D1FAE5','FEF3C7','EDE9FE'][i%4]}">${ti[c.type]||'📞'}</div><div style="flex:1"><strong>${c.name}</strong>${c.onQR?'<span style="font-size:.72rem;font-weight:700;padding:1px 7px;background:var(--rose-pale);color:var(--rose);border-radius:6px;margin-left:6px">🆘 QR</span>':''}<div style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-light)">${c.type}${c.notes?' · '+c.notes:''}</div><div style="font-size:.95rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--teal);margin-top:3px">${c.phone}</div>${c.addr?`<div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--slate-light)">${c.addr}</div>`:''}</div><div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:7px"><button class="call-btn" onclick="toast('📞 Calling ${c.name}...')">📞 Call</button>${caregiverMode?'':`<button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="editContact(${c.id})">✏️ Edit</button><button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="deleteContact(${c.id})">✕ Remove</button>`}</div></div>`).join('');
  el.innerHTML=`<div class="contact-card emergency"><div class="contact-avatar" style="background:#FEE2E2">🚑</div><div style="flex:1"><strong>Emergency Services</strong><div style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-light)">Police, Fire, Ambulance</div><div style="font-size:1.2rem;font-weight:800;color:#DC2626;margin-top:3px">911</div></div><button class="call-btn" style="background:#DC2626;font-size:1.1rem;padding:12px 20px" onclick="toast('📞 Calling 911...')">📞 Call 911</button></div><div class="contact-card"><div class="contact-avatar" style="background:#FEF3C7">☎️</div><div style="flex:1"><strong>Poison Control</strong><div style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-light)">24/7</div><div style="font-size:.95rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--teal);margin-top:3px">1-800-222-1222</div></div><button class="call-btn" onclick="toast('📞 Calling Poison Control...')">📞 Call</button></div>${custom}`;
}
function deleteContact(id){D.contacts=D.contacts.filter(c=>c.id!==id);save();renderAll();}

// Settings
function loadSettings(){
  const s = D.settings;
  if(s.name){ document.getElementById('set-name').value=s.name; document.getElementById('user-name-chip').textContent=s.name; }
  if(s.dob)   document.getElementById('set-dob').value   = s.dob;
  if(s.phone) document.getElementById('set-phone').value = s.phone;
  if(s.doc)   document.getElementById('set-doc').value   = s.doc;
  const blood = document.getElementById('set-blood');
  if(blood && s.blood) blood.value = s.blood;
  const da = document.getElementById('set-drug-allergies');
  if(da && s.drugAllergies)  da.value = s.drugAllergies;
  const fa = document.getElementById('set-food-allergies');
  if(fa && s.foodAllergies)  fa.value = s.foodAllergies;
  const oa = document.getElementById('set-other-allergies');
  if(oa && s.otherAllergies) oa.value = s.otherAllergies;
  // Populate conditions textarea (stored as plain string)
  const ca = document.getElementById('set-conditions');
  if(ca){
    const cval = typeof s.conditions==='string' ? s.conditions : (s.conditions||[]).join(', ');
    ca.value = cval;
  }
  renderConditions();
  renderAllergyPreviews(); // show pills immediately when settings load
}
function saveSettings(){
  D.settings = {
    ...D.settings,
    name:            document.getElementById('set-name').value,
    dob:             document.getElementById('set-dob').value,
    phone:           document.getElementById('set-phone').value,
    doc:             document.getElementById('set-doc').value,
    blood:           document.getElementById('set-blood')?.value || '',
    drugAllergies:   document.getElementById('set-drug-allergies')?.value || '',
    foodAllergies:   document.getElementById('set-food-allergies')?.value || '',
    otherAllergies:  document.getElementById('set-other-allergies')?.value || ''
  };
  save();
  if(D.settings.name) document.getElementById('user-name-chip').textContent = D.settings.name;
  toast('✅ Saved!', 'var(--sage)');
}
function exportData(){
  const exportPayload = {
    _meta: {
      version: 'tended-v1',
      exported: new Date().toISOString(),
      app: 'Tended Health Companion',
      counts: {
        meds: D.meds.length, appts: D.appts.length,
        health: D.health.length, symptoms: D.symptoms.length,
        claims: D.claims.length, docs: D.docs.length,
        contacts: D.contacts.length, family: D.family.length
      }
    },
    ...D
  };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(exportPayload, null, 2)], {type:'application/json'});
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const date = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  a.download = `tended-backup-${date}.json`;
  a.click();
  toast('✅ Backup saved! Keep this file somewhere safe.', 'var(--sage)');
}
function clearAllData(){if(!confirm('Delete ALL data?'))return;if(!confirm('Really? Cannot be undone.'))return;localStorage.clear();location.reload();}

function importData(input){
  const file = input.files[0];
  if(!file) return;
  const statusEl = document.getElementById('import-status');

  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = e => {
    try {
      const raw = JSON.parse(e.target.result);

      // Strip _meta wrapper if present (from our export format)
      const { _meta, ...data } = raw;

      // Validate it looks like Tended data
      const hasAnyData = data.meds || data.appts || data.health ||
                         data.symptoms || data.contacts || data.settings;
      if(!hasAnyData){
        showImportStatus('error', '❌ This file does not look like a Tended backup. Please select a valid tended-backup.json file.');
        return;
      }

      // Merge with defaults so missing keys don't break anything
      const defaults = {meds:[],appts:[],health:[],symptoms:[],claims:[],
                        docs:[],family:[],contacts:[],settings:{},
                        medChecks:{},notifications:[],prepChecks:{},checkins:[]};
      D = Object.assign(defaults, data);

      save();
      renderAll();
      loadSettings();
      loadDisplayMode();

      // Show summary of what was imported
      const counts = _meta?.counts || {
        meds: D.meds.length, appts: D.appts.length,
        health: D.health.length, symptoms: D.symptoms.length
      };
      const summary = [
        counts.meds     ? `${counts.meds} medication${counts.meds!==1?'s':''}` : null,
        counts.appts    ? `${counts.appts} appointment${counts.appts!==1?'s':''}` : null,
        counts.health   ? `${counts.health} health entr${counts.health!==1?'ies':'y'}` : null,
        counts.contacts ? `${counts.contacts} contact${counts.contacts!==1?'s':''}` : null,
      ].filter(Boolean).join(', ');

      const exportedOn = _meta?.exported
        ? ' — exported ' + new Date(_meta.exported).toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'})
        : '';

      showImportStatus('success', `✅ Import successful! Restored: ${summary || 'your data'}${exportedOn}`);
      toast('✅ Data restored successfully!', 'var(--sage)');

    } catch(err) {
      showImportStatus('error', '❌ Could not read file. Make sure it is a valid Tended backup (.json).');
    }
    // Reset input so same file can be re-selected
    input.value = '';
  };
  reader.readAsText(file);
}

function showImportStatus(type, msg){
  const el = document.getElementById('import-status');
  if(!el) return;
  el.style.display = 'block';
  el.style.background = type === 'success' ? 'var(--sage-pale)'  : 'var(--rose-pale)';
  el.style.border     = type === 'success' ? '1px solid #86EFAC' : '1px solid #FECACA';
  el.style.color      = type === 'success' ? 'var(--sage)'       : 'var(--rose)';
  el.textContent = msg;
  if(type === 'success') setTimeout(() => { el.style.display = 'none'; }, 6000);
}

// AI Chat
let chatHistory=[];
async function sendChat(){
  const input=document.getElementById('chat-input');const msg=input.value.trim();if(!msg)return;
  input.value='';appendMsg(msg,'user');
  const ctx=`Medications: ${D.meds.map(m=>m.name+(m.dose?' '+m.dose:'')).join(', ')||'none'}\nAppointments: ${D.appts.slice(0,3).map(a=>a.name+' on '+a.date).join(', ')||'none'}\nDoctor: ${D.settings.doc||'not specified'}`;
  const loadEl=appendMsg('','ai',true);chatHistory.push({role:'user',content:msg});
  try{const data=await apiFetch({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:1000,system:`You are a warm, patient health assistant for a senior adult. Help with medications, appointments, insurance, scam protection, and health questions.\n\n${ctx}\n\nBe clear, simple, safety-conscious. Keep responses to 2-4 paragraphs.`,messages:chatHistory});
    const reply=data.content?.[0]?.text||"I'm having trouble connecting. Please try again.";
    loadEl.remove();appendMsg(reply,'ai');chatHistory.push({role:'assistant',content:reply});if(chatHistory.length>20)chatHistory=chatHistory.slice(-20);
  }catch(e){loadEl.remove();if(e.message!=='NO_KEY'&&e.message!=='INVALID_KEY')appendMsg("I'm having trouble connecting. Please check your API key in Settings.","ai");}
}
function appendMsg(text,role,loading=false){const msgs=document.getElementById('chat-messages');const div=document.createElement('div');div.className='msg '+role+(loading?' loading':'');if(role==='ai'&&!loading)div.innerHTML=`<div class="ai-label">🤖 Tended AI</div>${text.replace(/\n/g,'<br>')}`;else if(loading)div.innerHTML='<div class="dots"><span></span><span></span><span></span></div>';else div.textContent=text;msgs.appendChild(div);msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;return div;}
function quickPrompt(btn){document.getElementById('chat-input').value=btn.textContent.trim();sendChat();}
async function generateDoctorQuestions(){
  const el=document.getElementById('doctor-questions');const btn=event.target;btn.disabled=true;btn.textContent='🤖 Generating…';el.innerHTML='<div style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:.88rem">Analyzing…</div>';
  const next=D.appts.find(a=>new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00')>=new Date());
  const ctx=`Meds: ${D.meds.map(m=>m.name+' '+m.dose).join(', ')||'none'}\nSymptoms: ${D.symptoms.slice(0,5).map(s=>s.symptoms.join(', ')).join('; ')||'none'}\nVitals: ${D.health[0]?`BP ${D.health[0].bp}, HR ${D.health[0].hr}`:'none'}\nNext appt: ${next?next.name:'-'}`;
  try{const data=await apiFetch({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:600,messages:[{role:'user',content:`Generate 6-8 smart doctor questions for this senior patient. Numbered list, plain language.\n\n${ctx}`}]});const text=data.content?.[0]?.text||'Unable to generate.';el.innerHTML=`<div style="background:var(--indigo-pale);border:1.5px solid #C7D2FE;border-radius:10px;padding:14px;font-size:.88rem;line-height:1.9;white-space:pre-wrap">${text}</div><button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm no-print" style="margin-top:10px" onclick="window.print()">🖨️ Print</button>`;}catch(e){if(e.message!=='NO_KEY'&&e.message!=='INVALID_KEY')el.innerHTML='<div style="color:var(--rose);font-size:.88rem">Unable to connect.</div>';}
  btn.disabled=false;btn.textContent='🤖 Generate Questions';
}

// Nav & Render
const BN_MAP={dashboard:'bn-dashboard',medications:'bn-medications',appointments:'bn-appointments',health:'bn-health'};
function navTo(id,btn,bnId){
  document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(s=>s.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.bn-item').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  const sec=document.getElementById('section-'+id);if(sec)sec.classList.add('active');
  if(btn)btn.classList.add('active');
  else document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(b=>{if(b.getAttribute('onclick')&&b.getAttribute('onclick').includes("'"+id+"'"))b.classList.add('active');});
  // Update bottom nav
  const bnKey=bnId||BN_MAP[id];
  if(bnKey){const bnEl=document.getElementById(bnKey);if(bnEl)bnEl.classList.add('active');}
  if(id==='vitals')setTimeout(renderVitalCharts,60);
  if(id==='timeline')setTimeout(()=>{renderMedTimeline();renderMedWeeklyChart();},60);
  if(id==='interactions')setTimeout(renderMyMedsList,60);
  if(id==='summary')setTimeout(buildSummaryPreview,60);
  if(id==='qr')setTimeout(()=>{if(D.settings.name)generateQrCard();},60);
  renderAll();document.querySelector('.content').scrollTop=0;
}
function navToMobile(id){toggleMobileMenu();navTo(id);}
function toggleMobileMenu(){
  const m=document.getElementById('mobile-menu');
  m.style.display=m.style.display==='none'?'block':'none';
}
function updateDashStats(){
  const today=new Date().toDateString();
  const done=D.meds.filter(m=>D.medChecks[m.id+'_'+today]).length,total=D.meds.length;
  document.getElementById('d-meds').textContent=done+'/'+total;
  document.getElementById('d-med-prog').style.width=(total?Math.round(done/total*100):0)+'%';
  const pending=D.claims.filter(c=>c.status==='pending'||c.status==='review').length;
  document.getElementById('d-claims').textContent=pending;document.getElementById('d-logs').textContent=D.health.length;
  document.getElementById('d-appts').textContent=D.appts.filter(a=>new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00')>=new Date(today)).length;
  const nb=document.getElementById('nb-meds'),rc=D.meds.filter(m=>m.refill&&(new Date(m.refill+'T00:00:00')-new Date())<7*86400000).length;
  if(rc>0){nb.textContent=rc;nb.style.display='inline';}else nb.style.display='none';
  // sync bottom nav badge
  const bnb=document.getElementById('bnb-meds');if(bnb)bnb.style.display=rc>0?'block':'none';
}
function renderAll(){
  renderDashMeds();renderAppts('d-appt-list',3);renderAppts('appts-full');
  renderMedsChecklist();renderMedsCards();renderHealth();renderSymptoms();
  renderClaims();renderDocs();renderFamily();renderContacts();
  renderPrepChecklist();renderMedTimeline();if(typeof Chart!=='undefined')renderVitalCharts();
  updateDashStats();updateHealthScore();renderCheckinStrip();renderMedicalAlert();
  // Keep SW schedule in sync
}

// Timeline
function renderMedTimeline(){
  const el=document.getElementById('med-timeline'),pEl=document.getElementById('med-pct-big');if(!el)return;
  const today=new Date().toDateString();
  if(!D.meds.length){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty"><div class="ei">⏰</div><p>Add medications with times.</p></div>';if(pEl)pEl.textContent='0%';return;}
  const sorted=[...D.meds].sort((a,b)=>{if(!a.time)return 1;if(!b.time)return-1;return parseTime(a.time)-parseTime(b.time);});
  const now=new Date(),nowMs=now.getHours()*3600000+now.getMinutes()*60000;
  el.innerHTML=sorted.map(m=>{const key=m.id+'_'+today;const chk=!!D.medChecks[key];const tMs=m.time?parseTime(m.time):null;const status=chk?'done':(tMs&&tMs<nowMs?'due':'upcoming');return`<div class="tl-slot"><div class="tl-time">${m.time||'—'}</div><div class="tl-dot ${status}"></div><div class="tl-content"><div class="tl-med">${m.name} ${m.dose?'· '+m.dose:''}</div><div class="tl-detail">${m.notes||m.freq||''} ${chk?'✓ Taken':status==='due'?'⚠️ Due now':''}</div></div><div class="check-box ${chk?'done':''}" onclick="toggleMedCheck('${key}')" style="flex-shrink:0">${chk?'✓':''}</div></div>`;}).join('');
  const done=D.meds.filter(m=>D.medChecks[m.id+'_'+today]).length;
  if(pEl)pEl.textContent=(D.meds.length?Math.round(done/D.meds.length*100):0)+'%';
  const sEl=document.getElementById('med-streak-display');
  if(sEl&&D.meds.length){let streak=0;for(let i=0;i<30;i++){const d=new Date();d.setDate(d.getDate()-i);const ds=d.toDateString();if(D.meds.filter(m=>D.medChecks[m.id+'_'+ds]).length===D.meds.length)streak++;else break;}sEl.innerHTML=`<div style="font-size:1.1rem;font-weight:700;color:${streak>=3?'var(--sage)':'var(--slate-light)'}">${streak>0?'🔥 '+streak+'-day streak!':'Start your streak today!'}</div>`;}
}
let weeklyChart=null;
function renderMedWeeklyChart(){
  if(typeof Chart === 'undefined') return;
  const canvas=document.getElementById('med-weekly-chart');if(!canvas)return;
  const sec=document.getElementById('section-timeline');if(!sec||!sec.classList.contains('active'))return;
  if(!D.meds.length)return;
  const days=[],pcts=[];for(let i=6;i>=0;i--){const d=new Date();d.setDate(d.getDate()-i);const ds=d.toDateString();const done=D.meds.filter(m=>D.medChecks[m.id+'_'+ds]).length;days.push(d.toLocaleDateString('en-US',{weekday:'short'}));pcts.push(D.meds.length?Math.round(done/D.meds.length*100):0);}
  if(weeklyChart){weeklyChart.destroy();weeklyChart=null;}
  weeklyChart=new Chart(canvas,{type:'bar',data:{labels:days,datasets:[{data:pcts,backgroundColor:pcts.map(p=>p>=80?'rgba(21,128,61,0.7)':p>=50?'rgba(245,158,11,0.7)':'rgba(190,18,60,0.6)'),borderRadius:6}]},options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{display:false}},scales:{y:{min:0,max:100,ticks:{callback:v=>v+'%',font:{size:10}},grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)'}},x:{ticks:{font:{size:10}},grid:{display:false}}}}});
}

// Vitals Charts
let vCharts={};
function renderVitalCharts(){
  if(typeof Chart === 'undefined') return; // Chart.js not loaded yet
  const sec=document.getElementById('section-vitals');if(!sec||!sec.classList.contains('active'))return;
  const entries=[...D.health].reverse().slice(-14);if(!entries.length)return;
  const labels=entries.map(e=>fmtDate(e.date).replace(/,\s*\d{4}/,''));
  function makeChart(id,label,data,color){const canvas=document.getElementById(id);if(!canvas)return;if(vCharts[id]){vCharts[id].destroy();delete vCharts[id];}const clean=data.map(v=>{const n=parseFloat(v);return isNaN(n)?null:n;});if(clean.every(v=>v===null))return;vCharts[id]=new Chart(canvas,{type:'line',data:{labels,datasets:[{label,data:clean,borderColor:color,backgroundColor:color+'22',borderWidth:2.5,pointRadius:4,pointBackgroundColor:color,tension:0.35,spanGaps:true}]},options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{display:false}},scales:{y:{ticks:{font:{size:10}},grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)'}},x:{ticks:{font:{size:9},maxRotation:30},grid:{display:false}}}}});}
  makeChart('bp-chart','Systolic BP',entries.map(e=>{if(!e.bp)return null;const m=e.bp.match(/^(\d+)/);return m?m[1]:null;}),'#0F766E');
  makeChart('hr-chart','Heart Rate',entries.map(e=>e.hr||null),'#EC4899');
  makeChart('wt-chart','Weight',entries.map(e=>e.wt||null),'#7C3AED');
  makeChart('bs-chart','Blood Sugar',entries.map(e=>e.bs||null),'#B45309');
}

// Prep Checklist
const PREP=['Confirm appointment time and location','Arrange transportation','Bring photo ID and insurance cards','Bring complete medication list','Write down symptoms and questions','Bring previous test results','Note any allergies','Charge phone before leaving'];
function renderPrepChecklist(){const el=document.getElementById('prep-checklist');if(!el)return;if(!D.prepChecks)D.prepChecks={};el.innerHTML=PREP.map((item,i)=>{const done=!!D.prepChecks['prep_'+i];return`<div class="prep-item"><div class="prep-check ${done?'done':''}" onclick="togglePrep(${i})">${done?'✓':''}</div><div style="font-size:.9rem;${done?'text-decoration:line-through;color:var(--slate-light)':''}">${item}</div></div>`;}).join('');}
function togglePrep(i){if(!D.prepChecks)D.prepChecks={};D.prepChecks['prep_'+i]=!D.prepChecks['prep_'+i];save();renderPrepChecklist();}

// Print Daily
function printDailyReport(){
  const today=new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US',{weekday:'long',year:'numeric',month:'long',day:'numeric'});
  const tds=new Date().toDateString();
  // Sort meds by time
  const timeToMin = t => {
    if(!t) return 9999;
    const m=t.match(/(\d+):(\d+)\s*(AM|PM)/i);
    if(!m) return 9999;
    let h=parseInt(m[1]),mn=parseInt(m[2]);
    if(m[3].toUpperCase()==='PM'&&h!==12) h+=12;
    if(m[3].toUpperCase()==='AM'&&h===12) h=0;
    return h*60+mn;
  };
  const sorted=[...D.meds].sort((a,b)=>timeToMin(a.time)-timeToMin(b.time));
  const medRows=sorted.map(m=>{
    const taken=D.medChecks[m.id+'_'+tds];
    return `<tr style="border-bottom:1px solid #E2D9CC">
      <td style="padding:10px 12px;font-size:1rem;font-weight:600">${m.name}</td>
      <td style="padding:10px 12px;color:#475569">${m.dose||'—'}</td>
      <td style="padding:10px 12px;color:#475569">${m.time||m.freq||'—'}</td>
      <td style="padding:10px 12px">${m.notes?`<span style="font-size:.82rem;color:#94A3B8">${m.notes}</span>`:''}</td>
      <td style="padding:10px 16px;text-align:center">
        <div style="width:28px;height:28px;border:2.5px solid ${taken?'#15803D':'#94A3B8'};border-radius:6px;display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;background:${taken?'#DCFCE7':'white'};font-size:1rem">${taken?'✓':''}</div>
      </td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="5" style="padding:16px;color:#94A3B8;text-align:center">No medications added</td></tr>';
  const name=D.settings.name||'My';
  const doc=D.settings.doc?`Dr. ${D.settings.doc}`:'';
  const vitals=D.health[0]?`BP: ${D.health[0].bp||'—'} &nbsp;·&nbsp; HR: ${D.health[0].hr||'—'} bpm &nbsp;·&nbsp; Weight: ${D.health[0].wt||'—'} lbs`:'Not yet recorded today';
  const w=window.open('','_blank');
  w.document.write(`<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><title>${name} — Medication Schedule</title><style>
    *{box-sizing:border-box;margin:0;padding:0}
    body{font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Arial,sans-serif;max-width:720px;margin:32px auto;color:#1E293B;font-size:15px;line-height:1.6;padding:0 20px}
    .header{border-bottom:3px solid #0F766E;padding-bottom:14px;margin-bottom:20px}
    .title{font-size:1.7rem;font-weight:700;color:#0F766E}
    .subtitle{font-size:.92rem;color:#475569;margin-top:4px}
    .meta{display:flex;gap:24px;margin-bottom:22px;flex-wrap:wrap}
    .meta-item{font-size:.88rem;color:#475569}
    .meta-item strong{color:#1E293B}
    table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:24px}
    thead{background:#F0FDF4}
    th{padding:10px 12px;text-align:left;font-size:.82rem;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.05em;color:#0F766E;border-bottom:2px solid #0F766E}
    th:last-child{text-align:center}
    .section-title{font-size:1rem;font-weight:700;color:#1E293B;margin-bottom:10px;border-bottom:1.5px solid #E2D9CC;padding-bottom:6px}
    .vitals-box{background:#F8FAFC;border:1.5px solid #E2D9CC;border-radius:10px;padding:12px 16px;font-size:.9rem;color:#475569;margin-bottom:22px}
    .footer{margin-top:32px;padding-top:12px;border-top:1px solid #E2D9CC;font-size:.75rem;color:#94A3B8;display:flex;justify-content:space-between}
    .instructions{background:#FFF7ED;border:1.5px solid #FED7AA;border-radius:10px;padding:12px 16px;font-size:.85rem;color:#92400E;margin-bottom:22px}
    @media print{body{margin:10px 16px}@page{size:A4;margin:15mm}}

}

function renderPinStatus(){
  const el=document.getElementById('pin-lock-status');const btn=document.getElementById('disable-pin-btn');if(!el)return;
  const set=localStorage.getItem(PIN_SET);
  const lb=document.getElementById('lock-now-btn');
  if(set==='1'){
    el.innerHTML='<span style="color:var(--sage)">🔒 PIN is enabled — app locks automatically</span>';
    if(btn)btn.style.display='inline-flex';
    if(lb)lb.style.display='flex';
  } else {
    el.innerHTML='<span style="color:var(--slate-light)">🔓 No PIN set — app opens without a lock</span>';
    if(btn)btn.style.display='none';
    if(lb)lb.style.display='none';
  }
}


// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FEATURE: ONBOARDING
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const OB_DONE_KEY = 'tendedOnboarded';
let _obStep = 0;

function obShow() {
  _obStep = 0;
  document.getElementById('ob-overlay').classList.add('open');
  obGoTo(0);
  // Hide biometric card on devices that don't support WebAuthn
  if (!window.PublicKeyCredential) {
    const card = document.getElementById('ob-bio-card');
    if (card) card.style.display = 'none';
  }
}

function obGoTo(n) {
  _obStep = n;
  document.querySelectorAll('.ob-step').forEach((s,i) => s.classList.toggle('active', i===n));
  document.querySelectorAll('.ob-dot').forEach((d,i) => d.classList.toggle('active', i===n));
  document.getElementById('ob-fill').style.width = ((n+1)/5*100)+'%';
}

function obNext(step, fieldId) {
  if (fieldId) {
    const val = document.getElementById(fieldId)?.value?.trim();
    if (val) { D.settings = {...D.settings, name: val}; save();
      document.getElementById('user-name-chip').textContent = val; }
  }
  obGoTo(step + 1);
}

function obSkip() {
  // On the security step, explicitly mark PIN as disabled so
  // the app never asks for one on next launch
  if(_obStep === 3){
    localStorage.setItem('tendedPinSet','disabled');
  }
  obGoTo(_obStep + 1);
}

function obSaveMed() {
  const name = document.getElementById('ob-med')?.value?.trim();
  if (name) {
    D.meds.push({ id: Date.now(), name,
      dose: document.getElementById('ob-dose')?.value || '',
      freq: 'Once daily',
      time: document.getElementById('ob-time')?.value || '',
      refill: '', doctor: '', notes: '' });
    save();
  }
  obGoTo(2);
}

function obSaveDoctor() {
  const doc = document.getElementById('ob-doc')?.value?.trim();
  const dob = document.getElementById('ob-dob')?.value;
  if (doc || dob) { D.settings = {...D.settings, doc: doc||'', dob: dob||''}; save(); }
  obGoTo(3);
}

function obSetPin() {
  document.getElementById('ob-overlay').classList.remove('open');
  localStorage.setItem(OB_DONE_KEY, '1');
  changePinFlow();
}

async function obSetBiometric() {
  const ok = await bioSetup();
  if (ok) obGoTo(4);
  else { toast('Biometric not available — set a PIN instead', 'var(--amber)'); }
}

function obFinish() {
  localStorage.setItem(OB_DONE_KEY, '1');
  document.getElementById('ob-overlay').classList.remove('open');
  renderAll(); loadSettings();
  showCheckinIfNeeded();
  // Start feature tour for new users
  setTimeout(tourStart, 600);
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FEATURE: BIOMETRIC UNLOCK (WebAuthn)
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const BIO_STORE = 'tendedBioId';

function bioAvailable() {
  return !!(window.PublicKeyCredential && navigator.credentials);
}

async function bioSetup() {
  if (!bioAvailable()) return false;
  try {
    const cred = await navigator.credentials.create({ publicKey: {
      challenge: crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(32)),
      rp: { name: 'Tended', id: location.hostname || 'localhost' },
      user: { id: new TextEncoder().encode('tended-user'), name: 'tended-user', displayName: 'Tended' },
      pubKeyCredParams: [{ alg: -7, type: 'public-key' }, { alg: -257, type: 'public-key' }],
      authenticatorSelection: { authenticatorAttachment: 'platform', userVerification: 'required' },
      timeout: 60000
    }});
    if (cred) {
      localStorage.setItem(BIO_STORE, btoa(String.fromCharCode(...new Uint8Array(cred.rawId))));
      localStorage.setItem('tendedBioOn', '1');
      toast('✅ Biometric unlock enabled!', 'var(--sage)');
      renderPinStatus();
      return true;
    }
  } catch(e) { if (e.name !== 'NotAllowedError') console.warn('Bio setup:', e.message); }
  return false;
}

async function bioUnlock() {
  if (!bioAvailable() || !localStorage.getItem('tendedBioOn')) return false;
  try {
    const idB64 = localStorage.getItem(BIO_STORE);
    const id = idB64 ? Uint8Array.from(atob(idB64), c => c.charCodeAt(0)) : null;
    const a = await navigator.credentials.get({ publicKey: {
      challenge: crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(32)),
      rpId: location.hostname || 'localhost',
      allowCredentials: id ? [{ id, type: 'public-key' }] : [],
      userVerification: 'required', timeout: 60000
    }});
    if (a) { unlockApp(null); return true; }
  } catch(e) { if (e.name !== 'NotAllowedError') console.warn('Bio unlock:', e.message); }
  return false;
}

function bioDisable() {
  localStorage.removeItem('tendedBioOn');
  localStorage.removeItem(BIO_STORE);
  toast('Biometric removed', 'var(--slate)');
  renderPinStatus();
}

function toggleDark() {
  const on = document.body.classList.toggle('dark-mode');
  D.settings.displayDark = on; save();
  const btn = document.getElementById('dark-toggle-btn');
  if (btn) btn.textContent = on ? '☀️' : '🌙';
  const cb = document.getElementById('toggle-dark');
  if (cb) cb.checked = on;
}
function syncDarkBtn() {
  const btn = document.getElementById('dark-toggle-btn');
  if (btn) btn.textContent = document.body.classList.contains('dark-mode') ? '☀️' : '🌙';
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FEATURE: SWIPE TO DELETE
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function initSwipe(selector) {
  document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach(wrap => {
    if (wrap._sw) return;
    wrap._sw = true;
    const inner = wrap.querySelector('.sw-inner');
    if (!inner) return;
    let sx = 0, sy = 0, drag = false;
    const start = (x, y) => { sx = x; sy = y; drag = true; };
    const move  = (x, y) => {
      if (!drag) return;
      const dx = x-sx, dy = y-sy;
      if (Math.abs(dy) > Math.abs(dx) && Math.abs(dy) > 8) { drag = false; return; }
      if (dx < -24) wrap.classList.add('open');
      if (dx >  24) wrap.classList.remove('open');
    };
    const end = () => { drag = false; };
    inner.addEventListener('touchstart', e => start(e.touches[0].clientX, e.touches[0].clientY), { passive: true });
    inner.addEventListener('touchmove',  e => move(e.touches[0].clientX, e.touches[0].clientY), { passive: true });
    inner.addEventListener('touchend', end);
    inner.addEventListener('mousedown', e => start(e.clientX, e.clientY));
    document.addEventListener('mousemove', e => { if (drag) move(e.clientX, e.clientY); });
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', end);
    document.addEventListener('click', e => { if (!wrap.contains(e.target)) wrap.classList.remove('open'); });
  });
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FEATURE: MED PHOTO SCANNER
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function scanOpen() {
  document.getElementById('scan-api-warn').style.display = getApiKey() ? 'none' : 'block';
  document.getElementById('scan-result').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('scan-img').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('scan-status').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('scan-overlay').classList.add('open');
}
function scanClose() {
  document.getElementById('scan-overlay').classList.remove('open');
  document.getElementById('scan-input').value = '';
}
async function scanPhoto(input) {
  const file = input.files[0]; if (!file) return;
  const img = document.getElementById('scan-img');
  const status = document.getElementById('scan-status');
  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = async e => {
    img.src = e.target.result; img.style.display = 'block';
    status.style.display = 'block'; status.textContent = '🤖 Reading label…';
    const b64 = e.target.result.split(',')[1];
    try {
      const data = await apiFetch({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 300,
        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: [
          { type: 'image', source: { type: 'base64', media_type: file.type||'image/jpeg', data: b64 } },
          { type: 'text', text: 'Read this medication label. Reply ONLY: NAME: value\nDOSE: value\nFREQ: value\nINSTR: value. Use Unknown if unclear.' }
        ]}]
      });
      const txt = data.content?.[0]?.text || '';
      document.getElementById('scan-name').value = txt.match(/NAME:\s*(.+)/i)?.[1]?.trim() || '';
      document.getElementById('scan-dose').value = (txt.match(/DOSE:\s*(.+)/i)?.[1]?.trim()||'').replace(/Unknown/i,'');
      document.getElementById('scan-freq').value = (txt.match(/FREQ:\s*(.+)/i)?.[1]?.trim()||'Once daily').replace(/Unknown/i,'Once daily');
      document.getElementById('scan-notes').value = (txt.match(/INSTR:\s*(.+)/i)?.[1]?.trim()||'').replace(/Unknown|none/i,'');
      status.style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('scan-result').style.display = 'block';
    } catch(err) {
      status.innerHTML = '<span style="color:var(--rose)">❌ Could not read label. Try better lighting.</span>';
    }
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(file);
}
function scanAdd() {
  const name = document.getElementById('scan-name').value.trim();
  if (!name) { toast('Please enter a name', 'var(--amber)'); return; }
  D.meds.push({ id: Date.now(), name,
    dose: document.getElementById('scan-dose').value,
    freq: document.getElementById('scan-freq').value || 'Once daily',
    time: '', refill: '', doctor: '',
    notes: document.getElementById('scan-notes').value });
  save(); scanClose(); renderAll();
  toast('✅ Medication added from label!', 'var(--sage)');
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FEATURE: VISIT PREP MODE
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function vpOpen() {
  const next = D.appts.find(a => new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00') >= new Date(new Date().toDateString()));
  const lbl = document.getElementById('vp-appt-label');

  // Appointment block
  const ai = document.getElementById('vp-appt-info');
  if (next) {
    const days = Math.ceil((new Date(next.date+'T00:00:00') - new Date(new Date().toDateString())) / 86400000);
    if (lbl) lbl.textContent = days === 0 ? 'Today!' : days === 1 ? 'Tomorrow' : `In ${days} days`;
    ai.innerHTML = `<div class="vp-title">📅 Appointment</div>
      <div style="background:var(--indigo-pale);border:1.5px solid #C7D2FE;border-radius:12px;padding:14px;font-size:.88rem;line-height:2">
        <strong>${next.name}</strong>${next.type?' — '+next.type:''}<br>
        ${next.date ? '📅 '+fmtDate(next.date)+(next.time?' at '+fmtTime(next.time):'') : ''}
        ${next.loc ? '<br>📍 '+next.loc : ''}
        ${next.transport ? '<br>🚗 '+next.transport : ''}
      </div>`;
  } else {
    if (lbl) lbl.textContent = 'No upcoming appointments';
    ai.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:.87rem">No upcoming appointments scheduled.</div>';
  }

  // Medications
  const medsEl = document.getElementById('vp-meds');
  medsEl.innerHTML = D.meds.length
    ? D.meds.map(m=>`<div class="vp-row"><div style="flex:1"><strong>${m.name}</strong>${m.dose?' '+m.dose:''}</div><div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--slate-light)">${m.freq||''}${m.time?' · '+m.time:''}</div></div>`).join('')
    : '<div style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:.87rem">No medications added.</div>';

  // Vitals (last 3)
  const vitalsEl = document.getElementById('vp-vitals');
  const rv = D.health.slice(0,3);
  vitalsEl.innerHTML = rv.length
    ? rv.map(h=>`<div class="vp-row"><div style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--slate-light);min-width:80px">${fmtDate(h.date)}</div><div style="flex:1;font-size:.84rem;display:flex;gap:12px;flex-wrap:wrap">${h.bp?`<span>🩺 ${h.bp}</span>`:''}${h.hr?`<span>💓 ${h.hr} bpm</span>`:''}${h.wt?`<span>⚖️ ${h.wt} lbs</span>`:''}${h.feel?`<span>${['','😞','😕','😐','🙂','😄'][h.feel]} ${h.feel}/5</span>`:''}</div></div>`).join('')
    : '<div style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:.87rem">No vitals logged.</div>';

  // Symptoms (last 2 weeks)
  const symsEl = document.getElementById('vp-syms');
  const rs = D.symptoms.filter(s=>(Date.now()-new Date(s.dt))<14*86400000).slice(0,5);
  symsEl.innerHTML = rs.length
    ? rs.map(s=>`<div class="vp-row"><div style="flex:1">${s.symptoms.join(', ')}</div><span style="font-size:.74rem;font-weight:700;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:6px;background:${s.severity==='severe'?'var(--rose-pale)':s.severity==='moderate'?'var(--amber-pale)':'var(--sage-pale)'};color:${s.severity==='severe'?'var(--rose)':s.severity==='moderate'?'var(--amber)':'var(--sage)'}">${s.severity}</span></div>`).join('')
    : '<div style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:.87rem">No symptoms in last 2 weeks.</div>';

  // Checklist
  const CL = ['Confirm appointment time & location','Arrange transportation','Bring photo ID and insurance cards',
    'Print or bring this health summary','Fast if blood work is required','Charge phone before leaving',
    'Note any new symptoms','Bring list of all current medications'];
  document.getElementById('vp-checklist').innerHTML = CL.map((item,i)=>
    `<div class="vp-row"><div class="vp-chk" id="vpc${i}" onclick="vpChk(${i},'vpc${i}')"></div><div style="font-size:.87rem">${item}</div></div>`).join('');

  document.getElementById('vp-questions').innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:.87rem">Tap Generate for AI-suggested questions.</div>';
  document.getElementById('vp-overlay').classList.add('open');
}

function vpClose() { document.getElementById('vp-overlay').classList.remove('open'); }

function vpChk(i, id) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  el.classList.toggle('done');
  el.textContent = el.classList.contains('done') ? '✓' : '';
}

async function vpGenQuestions() {
  const el = document.getElementById('vp-questions');
  el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--slate-light);font-size:.87rem">🤖 Generating…</div>';
  const meds = D.meds.map(m=>m.name+(m.dose?' '+m.dose:'')).join(', ')||'none';
  const syms = D.symptoms.slice(0,5).map(s=>s.symptoms.join(', ')+' ('+s.severity+')').join('; ')||'none';
  const vitals = D.health[0] ? `BP: ${D.health[0].bp||'?'}, HR: ${D.health[0].hr||'?'} bpm` : 'none';
  try {
    const data = await apiFetch({ model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: 450,
      messages: [{ role: 'user', content: `Generate 6-8 smart doctor questions for a senior patient.\nMedications: ${meds}\nSymptoms: ${syms}\nVitals: ${vitals}\nRespond with numbered list only, plain language.` }]
    });
    const txt = data.content?.[0]?.text || 'Unable to generate.';
    el.innerHTML = `<div style="background:var(--indigo-pale);border:1.5px solid #C7D2FE;border-radius:10px;padding:14px;font-size:.87rem;line-height:1.9;white-space:pre-wrap">${txt}</div>`;
  } catch(e) {
    if (e.message!=='NO_KEY'&&e.message!=='INVALID_KEY')
      el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--rose);font-size:.87rem">Unable to connect. Check API key in Settings.</div>';
  }
}

// FEATURE TOUR
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const TOUR_KEY = 'tendedTourDone';
let _tourStep  = 0;
let _tourActive = false;

const TOUR_STEPS = [
  {
    targetId: 'tour-target-meds',

    tip:      '💡 Set a PIN to protect your health information with a 4-digit lock.',
    label:    'Step 5 of 5',
    isLast:   true
  }
];

function tourStart() {
  if(localStorage.getItem(TOUR_KEY)) return; // already done
  _tourStep  = 0;
  _tourActive = true;
  document.getElementById('tour-backdrop').classList.add('active');
  tourRender();
}

function tourRender() {
  const step = TOUR_STEPS[_tourStep];
  if(!step) { tourDone(); return; }

  // Navigate to the section so the target element is visible
  navTo(step.section);
  setTimeout(() => {
    _doTourRender(step);
  }, 280); // wait for section transition
}

function _doTourRender(step) {
  // Find target element
  const target = step.targetId ? document.getElementById(step.targetId) : null;
  const spotlight = document.getElementById('tour-spotlight');
  const card      = document.getElementById('tour-card');

  // Update card content
  document.getElementById('tour-label').textContent = step.label;
  document.getElementById('tour-icon').textContent  = step.icon;
  document.getElementById('tour-title').textContent = step.title;
  document.getElementById('tour-body').textContent  = step.body;
  const tipEl = document.getElementById('tour-tip');
  if(step.tip){ tipEl.textContent = step.tip; tipEl.style.display = 'block'; }
  else { tipEl.style.display = 'none'; }

  // Dots
  const dotsEl = document.getElementById('tour-dots');
  dotsEl.innerHTML = TOUR_STEPS.map((_,i) =>
    `<div class="tour-dot${i===_tourStep?' active':''}"></div>`
  ).join('');

  // Next/Done button
  const nextBtn = document.getElementById('tour-next-btn');
  nextBtn.textContent = step.isLast ? '✓ Got it!' : 'Next →';

  // Position spotlight on target
  if(target) {
    const r = target.getBoundingClientRect();
    const pad = 8;
    spotlight.style.display = 'block';
    spotlight.style.left    = (r.left - pad) + 'px';
    spotlight.style.top     = (r.top  - pad) + 'px';
    spotlight.style.width   = (r.width  + pad*2) + 'px';
    spotlight.style.height  = (r.height + pad*2) + 'px';

    // Position card below or above the spotlight
    card.style.display = 'block';
    const cardW = Math.min(300, window.innerWidth - 48);
    let cardLeft = r.left;
    let cardTop  = r.bottom + pad + 14;

    // Flip above if card would go off bottom
    if(cardTop + 260 > window.innerHeight) {
      cardTop = r.top - pad - 260;
    }
    // Keep card within horizontal bounds
    if(cardLeft + cardW > window.innerWidth - 16) {
      cardLeft = window.innerWidth - cardW - 16;
    }
    if(cardLeft < 16) cardLeft = 16;

    card.style.left = cardLeft + 'px';
    card.style.top  = cardTop  + 'px';
    card.style.right = 'auto';
    card.style.bottom = 'auto';
  } else {
    // No target found — center the card
    spotlight.style.display = 'none';
    card.style.display = 'block';
    card.style.left   = '50%';
    card.style.top    = '50%';
    card.style.right  = 'auto';
    card.style.bottom = 'auto';
    card.style.transform = 'translate(-50%,-50%)';
  }
}

function tourNext() {
  _tourStep++;
  if(_tourStep >= TOUR_STEPS.length) { tourDone(); return; }
  // Reset transform in case it was centered
  document.getElementById('tour-card').style.transform = '';
  tourRender();
}

function tourSkip() { tourDone(); }

function tourDone() {
  _tourActive = false;
  localStorage.setItem(TOUR_KEY, '1');
  document.getElementById('tour-backdrop').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('tour-spotlight').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('tour-card').style.display = 'none';
  // Return to dashboard
  navTo('dashboard');
}

// Handle window resize during tour
window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
  if(_tourActive && TOUR_STEPS[_tourStep]) {
    _doTourRender(TOUR_STEPS[_tourStep]);
  }
});


// ── Offline / Online detection ────────────────────────────
function updateOnlineStatus(){
  const banner = document.getElementById('offline-banner');
  if(!banner) return;
  if(!navigator.onLine){
    banner.textContent = '📵 You\'re offline — your data is safe and the app still works';
    banner.className = 'show';
    banner.style.background = '#1E293B';
  } else {
    // Show brief "back online" confirmation then hide
    banner.textContent = '✅ Back online';
    banner.className = 'show online';
    setTimeout(() => { banner.className = ''; }, 3000);
  }
}
window.addEventListener('offline', updateOnlineStatus);
window.addEventListener('online',  updateOnlineStatus);
// Check on load
if(!navigator.onLine) updateOnlineStatus();


// ── Blood Pressure Trend Alert ────────────────────────────────
function checkBpAlert(){
  if(D.health.length < 3) return;
  const recent = D.health.slice(0,3);
  const highs = recent.filter(h=>{
    if(!h.bp) return false;
    const m = h.bp.match(/^(\d+)/);
    return m && parseInt(m[1]) >= 140;
  });
  if(highs.length >= 3){
    const alertKey = 'bp_alert_' + new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    if(!D.medChecks[alertKey]){
      D.medChecks[alertKey] = true; save();
      addNotif('🩺','Blood pressure alert',
        'Your last 3 readings have been 140 or above — consider calling your doctor.');
      // Show prominent dashboard warning
      const el = document.getElementById('bp-trend-alert');
      if(el) el.style.display = 'flex';
    }
  } else {
    const el = document.getElementById('bp-trend-alert');
    if(el) el.style.display = 'none';
  }
}




// ── Search / Filter ───────────────────────────────────────────
function filterMeds(q){
  const clear=document.getElementById('med-search-clear');
  if(clear) clear.style.display=q?'block':'none';
  const grid=document.getElementById('meds-cards');
  if(!q.trim()){renderMedsCards();return;}
  const lq=q.toLowerCase();
  const filtered=D.meds.filter(m=>(m.name+m.dose+m.freq+m.doctor+m.notes).toLowerCase().includes(lq));
  if(!filtered.length){grid.innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--slate-light)">No medications match your search.</p>';return;}
  const fe=[...D.meds];D.meds=filtered;renderMedsCards();D.meds=fe;
}
function clearMedSearch(){
  const inp=document.getElementById('med-search-input');
  if(inp){inp.value='';inp.focus();}
  const clear=document.getElementById('med-search-clear');
  if(clear) clear.style.display='none';
  renderMedsCards();
}

function filterHealth(q){
  const clear=document.getElementById('health-search-clear');
  if(clear) clear.style.display=q?'block':'none';
  const el=document.getElementById('health-entries');
  if(!q.trim()){renderHealth();return;}
  const lq=q.toLowerCase();
  const filtered=D.health.filter(h=>(h.date+h.bp+h.hr+h.wt+h.bs+h.notes).toLowerCase().includes(lq));
  if(!filtered.length){el.innerHTML='<p style="color:var(--slate-light)">No entries match your search.</p>';return;}
  const fe=[...D.health];D.health=filtered;renderHealth();D.health=fe;
}
function clearHealthSearch(){
  const inp=document.getElementById('health-search-input');
  if(inp){inp.value='';inp.focus();}
  const clear=document.getElementById('health-search-clear');
  if(clear) clear.style.display='none';
  renderHealth();
}


// ── Doctor Summary Export ─────────────────────────────────────
function printDoctorSummary(){
  const name = D.settings.name || 'Patient';
  const dob  = D.settings.dob  || 'Not set';
  const doc  = D.settings.doc  || 'Not specified';
  const phone= D.settings.phone|| '';
  const today= new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US',{year:'numeric',month:'long',day:'numeric'});

  // Medications
  const medRows = D.meds.map(m=>`
    <tr>
      <td>${m.name}</td><td>${m.dose||'—'}</td>
      <td>${m.freq||'—'}</td><td>${m.time||'—'}</td>
      <td>${m.doctor||'—'}</td><td>${m.notes||''}</td>
    </tr>`).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="6" style="color:#94A3B8">None recorded</td></tr>';

  // Recent vitals (last 5)
  const vitalRows = D.health.slice(0,5).map(h=>`
    <tr>
      <td>${h.date}</td><td>${h.bp||'—'}</td><td>${h.hr||'—'}</td>
      <td>${h.wt||'—'}</td><td>${h.bs||'—'}</td>
      <td>${h.o2||'—'}</td><td>${h.temp||'—'}</td>
      <td>${['','😞','😕','😐','🙂','😄'][h.feel]||'—'}</td>
    </tr>`).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="8" style="color:#94A3B8">No vitals recorded</td></tr>';

  // Recent symptoms (last 2 weeks)
  const twoWksAgo = Date.now() - 14*86400000;
  const recentSyms = D.symptoms.filter(s=>new Date(s.dt)>=twoWksAgo);
  const symRows = recentSyms.map(s=>`
    <tr>
      <td>${new Date(s.dt).toLocaleDateString()}</td>
      <td>${s.symptoms.join(', ')}</td>
      <td><span style="padding:1px 8px;border-radius:5px;font-size:.82rem;background:${s.severity==='severe'?'#FFF1F2':s.severity==='moderate'?'#FEF3C7':'#F0FDF4'};color:${s.severity==='severe'?'#BE123C':s.severity==='moderate'?'#B45309':'#15803D'}">${s.severity}</span></td>
      <td>${s.notes||''}</td>
    </tr>`).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="4" style="color:#94A3B8">No symptoms in past 2 weeks</td></tr>';

  // Upcoming appointments
  const upcomingAppts = D.appts
    .filter(a=>new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00')>=new Date(new Date().toDateString()))
    .slice(0,5)
    .map(a=>`<tr><td>${a.date}</td><td>${a.name}</td><td>${a.type||'—'}</td><td>${a.time?fmtTime(a.time):'—'}</td><td>${a.loc||'—'}</td></tr>`)
    .join('') || '<tr><td colspan="5" style="color:#94A3B8">None scheduled</td></tr>';

  const w = window.open('','_blank');
  w.document.write(`<!DOCTYPE html><html><head>
    <title>Doctor Summary — ${name}</title>
    <style>
      *{box-sizing:border-box;margin:0;padding:0}
      body{font-family:'Helvetica Neue',Arial,sans-serif;font-size:13px;color:#1E293B;line-height:1.5;padding:24px 32px}
      .header{display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;border-bottom:3px solid #0F766E;padding-bottom:14px;margin-bottom:18px}
      .patient-name{font-size:1.5rem;font-weight:700;color:#0F766E}
      .patient-meta{font-size:.85rem;color:#475569;margin-top:4px;line-height:1.8}
      .doc-info{text-align:right;font-size:.85rem;color:#475569}
      h2{font-size:.9rem;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;color:#475569;margin:18px 0 8px;padding-bottom:4px;border-bottom:1.5px solid #E2D9CC}
      table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:.83rem}
      th{background:#F8FAFC;text-align:left;padding:7px 10px;font-size:.75rem;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.04em;color:#475569;border-bottom:2px solid #E2D9CC}
      td{padding:7px 10px;border-bottom:1px solid #F1F5F9;vertical-align:top}
      tr:last-child td{border-bottom:none}
      .footer{margin-top:24px;padding-top:10px;border-top:1px solid #E2D9CC;font-size:.72rem;color:#94A3B8;display:flex;justify-content:space-between}
      .disclaimer{background:#FFF7ED;border:1px solid #FED7AA;border-radius:8px;padding:10px 14px;font-size:.78rem;color:#92400E;margin-top:16px}
      @media print{body{padding:10px 16px}@page{size:A4;margin:12mm}}
    
/* ── MEDICAL ALERT CARD ─────────────────────────────── */
