// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CAREGIVER DAILY TEXT SUMMARY
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function openDailySummary(){
  refreshDailySummary();
  openModal('daily-summary-modal');
}

function refreshDailySummary(){
  const inclMeds   = document.getElementById('ds-meds')?.checked   ?? true;
  const inclVitals = document.getElementById('ds-vitals')?.checked ?? true;
  const inclAppts  = document.getElementById('ds-appts')?.checked  ?? true;
  const inclFeel   = document.getElementById('ds-feel')?.checked   ?? true;

  const name  = D.settings.name || 'I';
  const today = new Date();
  const todayStr = today.toLocaleDateString('en-US',{weekday:'long',month:'long',day:'numeric'});
  const todayKey = today.toDateString();

  let lines = [];
  lines.push(`🏡 Tended Daily Update — ${todayStr}`);
  lines.push('');

  // Medications
  if(inclMeds && D.meds.length){
    const taken   = D.meds.filter(m => D.medChecks?.[`${m.id}_${todayKey}`]);
    const skipped = D.meds.filter(m => !D.medChecks?.[`${m.id}_${todayKey}`]);
    lines.push('💊 Medications:');
    D.meds.forEach(m => {
      const done = D.medChecks?.[`${m.id}_${todayKey}`];
      lines.push(`  ${done ? '✓' : '○'} ${m.name}${m.dose ? ' ' + m.dose : ''}${m.time ? ' (' + m.time + ')' : ''}`);
    });
    if(taken.length === D.meds.length){
      lines.push('  ✅ All medications taken!');
    } else if(taken.length > 0){
      lines.push(`  ${taken.length}/${D.meds.length} taken so far`);
    } else {
      lines.push('  None checked off yet today');
    }
    lines.push('');
  }

  // Vitals
  if(inclVitals && D.health.length){
    const lv = D.health[0];
    const feelMap = {5:'😄 Great',4:'🙂 Good',3:'😐 Okay',2:'😕 Not great',1:'😞 Rough day'};
    lines.push('❤️ Latest Vitals' + (lv.date !== today.toISOString().split('T')[0] ? ` (${fmtDate(lv.date)})` : '') + ':');
    if(lv.bp)   lines.push(`  Blood Pressure: ${lv.bp}`);
    if(lv.hr)   lines.push(`  Heart Rate: ${lv.hr} bpm`);
    if(lv.wt)   lines.push(`  Weight: ${lv.wt} lbs`);
    if(lv.bs)   lines.push(`  Blood Sugar: ${lv.bs} mg/dL`);
    if(lv.o2)   lines.push(`  Oxygen: ${lv.o2}%`);
    if(inclFeel && lv.feel) lines.push(`  Feeling: ${feelMap[lv.feel] || ''}`);
    if(lv.notes) lines.push(`  Note: ${lv.notes}`);
    lines.push('');
  } else if(inclFeel){
    // No vitals but include feeling if today's check-in exists
    lines.push('');
  }

  // Upcoming appointment
  if(inclAppts && D.appts.length){
    const next = D.appts.find(a => new Date(a.date+'T00:00:00') >= new Date(today.toDateString()));
    if(next){
      const daysAway = Math.ceil((new Date(next.date+'T00:00:00') - new Date(today.toDateString())) / 86400000);
      const when = daysAway === 0 ? 'Today' : daysAway === 1 ? 'Tomorrow' : `In ${daysAway} days (${fmtDate(next.date)})`;
      lines.push('📅 Next Appointment:');
      lines.push(`  ${when} — ${next.name}${next.type ? ', ' + next.type : ''}`);
      if(next.time) lines.push(`  Time: ${fmtTime(next.time)}`);
      if(next.loc)  lines.push(`  Location: ${next.loc}`);
      lines.push('');
    }
  }

  // Sign-off
  lines.push(`Sent from Tended — ${name}'s health app 🏡`);

  const text = lines.join('\n');
  const ta = document.getElementById('daily-summary-text');
  const cc = document.getElementById('daily-summary-chars');
  if(ta) ta.value = text;
  if(cc) cc.textContent = `${text.length} characters`;
}

async function copyDailySummary(){
  const text = document.getElementById('daily-summary-text')?.value;
  if(!text) return;
  const btn = document.getElementById('ds-copy-btn');
  try {
    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    if(btn){ btn.textContent = '✅ Copied!'; btn.style.background = 'var(--sage)'; }
    setTimeout(()=>{
      if(btn){ btn.textContent = '📋 Copy to Clipboard'; btn.style.background = ''; }
    }, 2500);
    toast('✅ Summary copied — paste it into a text message!','var(--sage)');
  } catch(e){
    // Fallback: select the textarea
    const ta = document.getElementById('daily-summary-text');
    if(ta){ ta.select(); document.execCommand('copy'); }
    toast('Summary selected — press Ctrl+C to copy','var(--teal)');
  }
}


// ── Log Off ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
function logOff(){
  if(!confirm('Log out of Tended? Your data stays saved on this device.')) return;

  // Close every overlay
  ['ob-overlay','scan-overlay','vp-overlay','daily-summary-modal',
   'med-modal','appt-modal','health-modal','symptom-modal','contact-modal'
  ].forEach(id => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if(el) el.classList.remove('open');
  });
  document.getElementById('checkin-overlay').style.display = 'none';
  document.querySelectorAll('.overlay.open').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('open'));

  clearTimeout(lockTimer);

  // ── With PIN: show PIN entry screen ──────────────────────────
  if(localStorage.getItem(PIN_SET)==='1'){
    pinBuffer=''; pinMode='enter'; updateDots();
    document.getElementById('pin-title').textContent    = 'Tended';
    document.getElementById('pin-subtitle').textContent = 'Enter your PIN to continue';
    document.getElementById('pin-error').textContent    = '';
    document.getElementById('pin-forgot').style.display = 'block';
    document.getElementById('pin-skip-btn').style.display = 'none';
    const bioBtn = document.getElementById('pin-bio-btn');
    if(bioBtn) bioBtn.style.display = localStorage.getItem('tendedBioOn') ? 'block' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('pin-screen').style.display = 'flex';
    return;
  }

  // ── No PIN: show the logged-out screen ───────────────────────
  document.getElementById('logout-screen').style.display = 'flex';
}

function openFromLogout(){
  document.getElementById('logout-screen').style.display = 'none';
  // Bring up onboarding if first time, otherwise go straight to app
  const isNew = !localStorage.getItem(OB_DONE_KEY) && !D.meds.length && !D.appts.length;
  if(isNew){ obShow(); }
  else { showCheckinIfNeeded(); }
}


// ── Medical Conditions ────────────────────────────────────────
function addCondition(){
  const inp = document.getElementById('condition-input');
  const val = inp?.value.trim();
  if(!val) return;
  if(!D.settings.conditions) D.settings.conditions = [];
  if(!D.settings.conditions.includes(val)){
    D.settings.conditions.push(val);
    save();
    renderConditions();
    toast('✅ Condition added', 'var(--sage)');
  }
  inp.value = '';
}

function removeCondition(idx){
  if(!D.settings.conditions) return;
  D.settings.conditions.splice(idx, 1);
  save();
  renderConditions();
}

function renderConditions(){
  const el = document.getElementById('conditions-list');
  if(!el) return;
  const list = D.settings.conditions || [];
  if(!list.length){
    el.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:.85rem;color:var(--slate-light);margin-bottom:8px">No conditions added yet.</p>';
    return;
  }
  el.innerHTML = list.map((c,i) =>
    `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;background:var(--cream);border:1.5px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:8px 12px;margin-bottom:7px;font-size:.9rem">
      <span style="flex:1;color:var(--slate)">${c}</span>
      <button onclick="removeCondition(${i})" style="background:none;border:none;color:var(--slate-light);cursor:pointer;font-size:1rem;line-height:1;padding:2px" aria-label="Remove">✕</button>
    </div>`
  ).join('');
}


// ── Allergies ──────────────────────────────────────────────
function saveAllergies(){
  D.settings={...D.settings,
    drugAllergies:  (document.getElementById('set-drug-allergies')?.value||'').trim(),
    foodAllergies:  (document.getElementById('set-food-allergies')?.value||'').trim(),
    otherAllergies: (document.getElementById('set-other-allergies')?.value||'').trim()
  };
  save();
  toast('✅ Allergies saved!','var(--sage)');
}


// ── Medical Conditions ─────────────────────────────────────
function saveConditions(){
  D.settings={...D.settings,
    conditions: (document.getElementById('set-conditions')?.value||'').trim(),
    bloodType:  document.getElementById('set-blood-type')?.value||'',
    surgeries:  (document.getElementById('set-surgeries')?.value||'').trim()
  };
  save();
  toast('✅ Medical info saved!','var(--sage)');
}


// ── Medical Alert Dashboard Card ─────────────────────────────────────
function renderMedicalAlert(){
  const s = D.settings;
  const drug  = (s.drugAllergies||'').trim();
  const food  = (s.foodAllergies||'').trim();
  const other = (s.otherAllergies||'').trim();
  const cond  = (typeof s.conditions==='string' ? s.conditions : (s.conditions||[]).join(', ')).trim();
  const blood = (s.blood||s.bloodType||'').trim();

  const hasAllergy = drug||food||other;
  const hasAnything = hasAllergy || cond || blood;

  const card = document.getElementById('dash-medical-alert');
  if(!card) return;
  card.style.display = hasAnything ? 'block' : 'none';

  // Allergies section
  const allergySection = document.getElementById('dash-alert-allergies');
  const allergyText    = document.getElementById('dash-alert-allergy-text');
  if(hasAllergy){
    allergySection.style.display = 'block';
    const parts = [drug&&`💊 ${drug}`, food&&`🍽️ ${food}`, other&&`🌿 ${other}`].filter(Boolean);
    allergyText.className = 'alert-section-value';
    allergyText.textContent = parts.join(' · ');
  } else if(allergySection) {
    allergySection.style.display = 'none';
  }

  // Conditions section
  const condSection = document.getElementById('dash-alert-conditions');
  const condText    = document.getElementById('dash-alert-condition-text');
  if(condSection){
    condSection.style.display = cond ? 'block' : 'none';
    if(condText){ condText.className='alert-section-value'; condText.textContent=cond; }
  }

  // Blood type section
  const bloodSection = document.getElementById('dash-alert-blood');
  const bloodText    = document.getElementById('dash-alert-blood-text');
  if(bloodSection){
    bloodSection.style.display = blood ? 'block' : 'none';
    if(bloodText){ bloodText.className='alert-section-value'; bloodText.textContent=blood; }
  }
}

// ── Live pill previews in Settings ───────────────────────────────────
function previewAllergies(){
  const drug  = (document.getElementById('set-drug-allergies')?.value||'').trim();
  const food  = (document.getElementById('set-food-allergies')?.value||'').trim();
  const other = (document.getElementById('set-other-allergies')?.value||'').trim();
  const preview = document.getElementById('allergy-preview');
  const pills   = document.getElementById('allergy-pills');
  if(!preview||!pills) return;
  const all = [
    ...drug.split(',').map(s=>s.trim()).filter(Boolean),
    ...food.split(',').map(s=>s.trim()).filter(Boolean),
    ...other.split(',').map(s=>s.trim()).filter(Boolean)
  ];
  preview.style.display = all.length ? 'block' : 'none';
  pills.innerHTML = all.map(a=>`<span class="allergy-pill">⚠️ ${a}</span>`).join('');
}

function previewConditions(){
  const cond = (document.getElementById('set-conditions')?.value||'').trim();
  const preview = document.getElementById('conditions-preview');
  const pills   = document.getElementById('condition-pills');
  if(!preview||!pills) return;
  const all = cond.split(',').map(s=>s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  preview.style.display = all.length ? 'block' : 'none';
  pills.innerHTML = all.map(c=>`<span class="condition-pill">🏥 ${c}</span>`).join('');
}

function renderAllergyPreviews(){
  previewAllergies();
  previewConditions();
}

// Init
function init(){
  initPin();loadProfiles();
  // Set up dirty tracking on all modals
  ['med-modal','appt-modal','health-modal','symptom-modal','contact-modal'].forEach(id=>{
    const el=document.getElementById(id);if(!el)return;
    el.querySelectorAll('input,textarea,select').forEach(inp=>{
      inp.addEventListener('input',()=>markModalDirty(id));
      inp.addEventListener('change',()=>markModalDirty(id));
    });
    el.addEventListener('click',e=>{if(e.target===el)closeModal(id);});
  });
  const now=new Date();
  document.getElementById('top-date').textContent=now.toLocaleDateString('en-US',{weekday:'long',month:'long',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'});
  const h=now.getHours();document.getElementById('greeting-time').textContent=h<12?'morning':h<17?'afternoon':'evening';
  const today=now.toISOString().split('T')[0];
  ['h-date','a-date'].forEach(id=>{const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.value=today;});
  const dt=document.getElementById('sy-dt');if(dt){const n=new Date();n.setMinutes(0,0,0);dt.value=n.toISOString().slice(0,16);}
  // Only show demo data if user explicitly asked (via button)
  // New users go through onboarding flow instead
  renderAll();
  loadSettings();loadDisplayMode();populateScamTips();renderKeyStatus();renderPinStatus();loadLockTimeout();
  // Show Skip button on first-time setup
  if(!localStorage.getItem(PIN_SET)){document.getElementById('pin-skip-btn').style.display='block';}
  checkRefillAlerts();checkApptAlerts();renderNotifBadge();checkBpAlert();
  syncDarkBtn();
  // Show tour for users who've onboarded but haven't seen the tour
  if(localStorage.getItem(OB_DONE_KEY) && !localStorage.getItem(TOUR_KEY)) {
    setTimeout(tourStart, 1200);
  }
}
init();


</script>
